<span data-ttu-id="15c79-375">O número de pacotes numa piscina de pacotes é uma função do tamanho da carga útil e do número total de bytes na área de memória fornecida à piscina de pacotes criar serviço.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-375">The number of packets in a packet pool is a function of the payload size and the total number of bytes in the memory area supplied to the packet pool create service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-376">A capacidade da piscina é calculada dividindo o tamanho do pacote (incluindo o tamanho do cabeçalho NX_PACKET, o tamanho da carga útil e o alinhamento adequado) no número total de bytes na área de memória fornecida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-376">The capacity of the pool is calculated by dividing the packet size (including the size of the NX_PACKET header, the payload size, and proper alignment) into the total number of bytes in the supplied memory area.</span></span>

### <a name="payload-area-alignment"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-377">Alinhamento da área de carga útil</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-377">Payload Area Alignment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-378">O design da piscina de pacotes no NetX Duo suporta cópia zero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-378">Packet pool design in NetX Duo supports zero-copy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-379">Ao nível do controlador do dispositivo, o controlador é capaz de atribuir a área de carga útil diretamente aos descritores tampão para a receção de dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-379">At the device driver level, the driver is able to assign the payload area directly into buffer descriptors for data reception.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-380">Por vezes, o motor DMA ou o mecanismo de sincronização de cache requerem que o endereço de partida da área de carga útil tenha um determinado requisito de alinhamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-380">Sometimes the DMA engine or the cache synchronization mechanism requires the starting address of the payload area to have a certain alignment requirement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-381">Isto pode ser conseguido definindo o requisito de alinhamento desejado (in bytes) em ***NX_PACKET_ALIGNMENT***.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-381">This can be achieved by defining the desired alignment requirement (in bytes) in ***NX_PACKET_ALIGNMENT***.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-382">Ao criar uma piscina de pacotes, o endereço inicial da área de carga útil irá alinhar-se a este valor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-382">When creating a packet pool, the starting address of the payload area will aligned to this value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-383">Por predefinição, o endereço inicial está alinhado com 4 bytes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-383">By default, starting address is 4-byte aligned.</span></span>

### <a name="thread-suspension"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-384">Suspensão do fio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-384">Thread Suspension</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-385">Os fios de aplicação podem suspender enquanto esperam por um pacote de uma piscina vazia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-385">Application threads can suspend while waiting for a packet from an empty pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-386">Quando um pacote é devolvido à piscina, o fio suspenso é dado este pacote e retomado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-386">When a packet is returned to the pool, the suspended thread is given this packet and resumed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-387">Se várias linhas forem suspensas na mesma piscina de pacotes, elas retomadas na ordem em que foram suspensas (FIFO).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-387">If multiple threads are suspended on the same packet pool, they  resumed in the order they were suspended (FIFO).</span></span>

### <a name="pool-statistics-and-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-388">Estatísticas e erros da piscina</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-388">Pool Statistics and Errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-389">Se ativado, o software de gestão de pacotes NetX Duo acompanha várias estatísticas e erros que podem ser úteis à aplicação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-389">If enabled, the NetX Duo packet management software keeps track of several statistics and errors that may be useful to the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-390">São mantidas as seguintes estatísticas e relatórios de erro para os pools de pacotes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-390">The following statistics and error reports are maintained for packet pools:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-391">Pacotes totais em piscina</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-391">Total Packets in Pool</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-392">Pacotes gratuitos na piscina</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-392">Free Packets in Pool</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-393">Total de dotações de pacotes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-393">Total Packet Allocations</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-394">Pedidos de atribuição vazios da piscina</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-394">Pool Empty Allocation Requests</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-395">Suspensões de atribuição vazias da piscina</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-395">Pool Empty Allocation Suspensions</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-396">Lançamentos de pacotes inválidos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-396">Invalid Packet Releases</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-397">Todas estas estatísticas e relatórios de erro, com exceção da contagem total e gratuita de pacotes na piscina, são incorporados na biblioteca NetX Duo, a menos que \***NX_DISABLE_PACKET_INFO** _ seja definido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-397">All of these statistics and error reports, except for total and free packet count in pool, are built into NetX Duo library unless \***NX_DISABLE_PACKET_INFO** _ is defined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-398">Estes dados estão disponíveis para a aplicação com o serviço _ *_nx_packet_pool_info_get*_\*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-398">This data is available to the application with the _ *_nx_packet_pool_info_get_*\* service.</span></span>

### <a name="packet-pool-control-block-nx_packet_pool"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-399">Bloco de controlo de piscina de pacote NX_PACKET_POOL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-399">Packet Pool Control Block NX_PACKET_POOL</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-400">As características de cada conjunto de memória de pacotes encontram-se no seu bloco de controlo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-400">The characteristics of each packet memory pool are found in its control block.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-401">Contém informações úteis, tais como a lista ligada de pacotes gratuitos, o número de pacotes gratuitos e o tamanho da carga útil para pacotes nesta piscina.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-401">It contains useful information such as the linked list of free packets, the number of free packets, and the payload size for packets in this pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-402">Esta estrutura é definida no ficheiro ***nx_api.h.***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-402">This structure is defined in the ***nx_api.h*** file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-403">Os blocos de controlo da piscina de pacote podem ser localizados em qualquer lugar da memória, mas é mais comum fazer do bloco de controlo uma estrutura global definindo-o fora do âmbito de qualquer função.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-403">Packet pool control blocks can be located anywhere in memory, but it is most common to make the control block a global structure by defining it outside the scope of any function.</span></span>

## <a name="ipv4-protocol"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-404">Protocolo IPv4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-404">IPv4 Protocol</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-405">O componente de Protocolo de Internet (IP) da NetX Duo é responsável pelo envio e receção de pacotes IPv4 na Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-405">The Internet Protocol (IP) component of NetX Duo is responsible for sending and receiving IPv4 packets on the Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-406">No NetX Duo, é o componente em última instância responsável pelo envio e receção de mensagens TCP, UDP, ICMP e IGMP, utilizando o controlador de rede subjacente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-406">In NetX Duo, it is the component ultimately responsible for sending and receiving TCP, UDP, ICMP, and IGMP messages, utilizing the underlying network driver.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-407">NetX Duo suporta o protocolo IPv4 (RFC 791) e o protocolo IPv6 (RFC 2460).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-407">NetX Duo supports both IPv4 protocol (RFC 791) and IPv6 protocol (RFC 2460).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-408">Esta secção discute o IPv4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-408">This section discusses IPv4.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-409">O IPv6 é discutido na próxima secção.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-409">IPv6 is discussed in the next section.</span></span>

### <a name="ipv4-addresses"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-410">Endereços IPv4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-410">IPv4 Addresses</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-411">Cada anfitrião na Internet tem um identificador único de 32 bits chamado endereço IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-411">Each host on the Internet has a unique 32-bit identifier called an IP address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-412">Existem cinco classes de endereços IPv4, conforme descrito na Figura 4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-412">There are five classes of IPv4 addresses as described in Figure 4.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-413">As gamas das cinco classes de endereços IPv4 são as seguintes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-413">The ranges of the five IPv4 address classes are as follows:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-414">Classe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-414">Class</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-415">Intervalo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-415">Range</span></span>|
|---|---|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-416">A</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-416">A</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-417">0.0.0.0 para 127.255.255.255</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-417">0.0.0.0 to 127.255.255.255</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-418">B</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-418">B</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-419">128.0.0.0 para 191.255.255.255</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-419">128.0.0.0 to 191.255.255.255</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-420">C</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-420">C</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-421">192.0.0.0 para 223.255.255.255</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-421">192.0.0.0 to 223.255.255.255</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-422">D</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-422">D</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-423">224.0.0.0 para 239.255.255.255</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-423">224.0.0.0 to 239.255.255.255</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-424">E</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-424">E</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-425">240.0.0.0 para 247.255.255.255</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-425">240.0.0.0 to 247.255.255.255</span></span>|

![Diagrama da Estrutura de Endereços IPv4.](./media/user-guide/ipv4-address-structure.png)

### <a name="figure-4-ipv4-address-structure"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-427">FIGURA 4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-427">FIGURE 4.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-428">Estrutura de endereços IPv4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-428">IPv4 Address Structure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-429">Existem também três tipos de especificações de endereços: *unicast,* *transmissão* e *multicast.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-429">There are also three types of address specifications: *unicast*, *broadcast*, and *multicast*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-430">Os endereços unicast são os endereços IPv4 que identificam um anfitrião específico na Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-430">Unicast addresses are those IPv4 addresses that identify a specific host on the Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-431">Os endereços Unicast podem ser uma fonte ou um endereço IPv4 de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-431">Unicast addresses can be either a source or a destination IPv4 address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-432">Um endereço de transmissão identifica todos os anfitriões numa rede ou sub-rede específica e só pode ser usado como endereços de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-432">A broadcast address identifies all hosts on a specific network or sub-network and can only be used as destination addresses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-433">Os endereços de transmissão são especificados tendo a parte de identificação do anfitrião do endereço definida para os outros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-433">Broadcast addresses are specified by having the host ID portion of the address set to ones.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-434">Endereços multicast (Classe D) especificam um grupo dinâmico de anfitriões na Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-434">Multicast addresses (Class D) specify a dynamic group of hosts on the Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-435">Os membros do grupo multicast podem juntar-se e sair quando quiserem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-435">Members of the multicast group may join and leave whenever they wish.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-436">*Apenas protocolos sem ligação como o UDP sobre o IPv4 podem utilizar a transmissão e a capacidade de transmissão limitada do grupo multicast.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-436">*Only connectionless protocols like UDP over IPv4 can utilize broadcast and the limited broadcast capability of the multicast group.*</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-437">\*O *IP_ADDRESS* macro é definido em \***nx_api.h** _.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-437">\*The macro *IP_ADDRESS* is defined in \***nx_api.h** _.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-438">Permite uma especificação fácil dos endereços IPv4 utilizando vírgulas em vez de um período.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-438">It allows easy specification of IPv4 addresses using commas instead of a periods.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-439">Por exemplo, _IP_ADDRESS (128,0,0,0)\* especifica o endereço da primeira classe B mostrado na Figura 4.\*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-439">For example, _IP_ADDRESS(128,0,0,0)\* specifies the first class B address shown in Figure 4.\*</span></span>

### <a name="ipv4-gateway-address"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-440">Endereço IPv4 Gateway</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-440">IPv4 Gateway Address</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-441">Os gateways de rede ajudam os anfitriões nas suas redes a transmitir pacotes destinados a destinos fora do domínio local.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-441">Network gateways assist hosts on their networks to relay packets destined to destinations outside the local domain.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-442">Cada nó tem algum conhecimento de qual próximo salto enviar para, seja o destino de um dos seus vizinhos, ou através de uma mesa de encaminhamento estático pré-programada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-442">Each node has some knowledge of which next hop to send to, either the destination one of its neighbors, or through a pre-programmed static routing table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-443">No entanto, se estas abordagens falharem, o nó deve encaminhar o pacote para o seu gateway predefinido, que tem um melhor conhecimento sobre como encaminhar o pacote para o seu destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-443">However if these approaches fail, the node should forward the packet to its default gateway which has better knowledge on how to route the packet to its destination.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-444">Note que o gateway predefinido deve ser diretamente acessível através de uma das interfaces físicas anexas à instância IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-444">Note that the default gateway must be directly accessible through one of the physical interfaces attached to the IP instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-445">A aplicação chama \***nx_ip_gateway_address_set** _ para configurar o endereço de gateway padrão IPv4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-445">The application calls \***nx_ip_gateway_address_set** _ to configure IPv4 default gateway address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-446">Utilize o _*_nx_ip_gateway_address_get_*_ de serviço para recuperar as atuais definições de gateway IPv4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-446">Use the service _*_nx_ip_gateway_address_get_*_ to retrieve the current IPv4 gateway settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-447">A aplicação deve utilizar o serviço _ *_nx_ip_gateway_address_clear_*\* para limpar a definição do gateway.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-447">Application shall use the service _ *_nx_ip_gateway_address_clear_*\* to clear the gateway setting.</span></span>

### <a name="ipv4-header"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-448">Cabeçalho IPv4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-448">IPv4 Header</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-449">Para que qualquer pacote IPv4 seja enviado na Internet, deve ter um cabeçalho IPv4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-449">For any IPv4 packet to be sent on the Internet, it must have an IPv4 header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-450">Quando os protocolos de nível superior (UDP, TCP, ICMP ou IGMP) ligam para o componente IP para enviar um pacote, o módulo de transmissão IPv4 coloca um cabeçalho IPv4 à frente dos dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-450">When higher-level protocols (UDP, TCP, ICMP, or IGMP) call the IP component to send a packet, the IPv4 transmit module places an IPv4 header in front of the data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-451">Inversamente, quando os pacotes IP são recebidos da rede, o componente IP remove o cabeçalho IPv4 do pacote antes da entrega aos protocolos de nível superior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-451">Conversely, when IP packets are received from the network, the IP component removes the IPv4 header from the packet before delivery to the higher-level protocols.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-452">A figura 5 mostra o formato do cabeçalho IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-452">Figure 5 shows the format of the IP header.</span></span>

![Formato iPv4 header](./media/user-guide/ipv4-header-format.png)

### <a name="figure-5-ipv4-header-format"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-454">FIGURA 5.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-454">FIGURE 5.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-455">Formato iPv4 header</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-455">IPv4 Header Format</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-456">*Espera-se que todos os cabeçalhos na implementação TCP/IP estejam em grande formato **endiano.** Neste formato, o byte mais significativo da palavra reside no endereço byte mais baixo. Por exemplo, a versão de 4 bits e o comprimento do cabeçalho de 4 bits do cabeçalho IP devem ser localizados no primeiro byte do cabeçalho.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-456">*All headers in the TCP/IP implementation are expected to be in **big endian** format. In this format, the most significant byte of the word resides at the lowest byte address. For example, the 4-bit version and the 4-bit header length of the IP header must be located on the first byte of the header.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-457">Os campos do cabeçalho IPv4 são definidos da seguinte forma:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-457">The fields of the IPv4 header are defined as follows:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-458">Campo de &nbsp; cabeçalho IPv4 &nbsp;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-458">IPv4&nbsp;Header&nbsp;Field</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-459">Objetivo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-459">Purpose</span></span> |
|---|---|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-460">***Versão de 4 bits***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-460">***4-bit version***</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-461">Este campo contém a versão de IP que este cabeçalho representa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-461">This field contains the version of IP this header represents.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-462">Para a versão IP 4, que é o que o NetX Duo suporta, o valor deste campo é 4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-462">For IP version 4, which is what NetX Duo supports, the value of this field is 4.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-463">***Comprimento do cabeçalho de 4 bits***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-463">***4-bit header length***</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-464">Este campo especifica o número de palavras de 32 bits no cabeçalho IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-464">This field specifies the number of 32-bit words in the IP header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-465">Se não houver palavras de opção, o valor para este campo é 5.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-465">If no option words are present, the value for this field is 5.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-466">***Tipo de serviço de 8 bits (TOS)***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-466">***8-bit type of service (TOS)***</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-467">Este campo especifica o tipo de serviço solicitado para este pacote IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-467">This field specifies the type of service requested for this IP packet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-468">Os pedidos válidos são os seguintes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-468">Valid requests are as follows:</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="15c79-469">- Normal: 0x00</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-469">- Normal: 0x00</span></span> <br /><span data-ttu-id="15c79-470">- Atraso mínimo: 0x00</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-470">- Minimum Delay: 0x00</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="15c79-471">- Dados Máximos: 0x08</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-471">- Maximum Data: 0x08</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="15c79-472">- Fiabilidade máxima: 0x04</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-472">- Maximum Reliability: 0x04</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="15c79-473">- Custo Mínimo: 0x02</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-473">- Minimum Cost: 0x02</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-474">***Comprimento total de 16 bits***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-474">***16-bit total length***</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-475">Este campo contém o comprimento total do datagrama IP em bytes, incluindo o cabeçalho IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-475">This field contains the total length of the IP datagram in bytes, including the IP header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-476">Um datagrama IP é a unidade básica de informação encontrada numa Internet TCP/IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-476">An IP datagram is the basic unit of information found on a TCP/IP Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-477">Contém um endereço de destino e origem para além dos dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-477">It contains a destination and source address in addition to data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-478">Por ser um campo de 16 bits, o tamanho máximo de um datagrama IP é de 65.535 bytes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-478">Because it is a 16-bit field, the maximum size of an IP datagram is 65,535 bytes.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-479">***Identificação de 16 bits***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-479">***16-bit identification***</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-480">O campo é um número usado para identificar exclusivamente cada datagrama IP enviado de um anfitrião.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-480">The field is a number used to uniquely identify each IP datagram sent from a host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-481">Este número é tipicamente incrementado após o envio de um datagrama IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-481">This number is typically incremented after an IP datagram is sent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-482">É especialmente útil na montagem de fragmentos de pacotes IP recebidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-482">It is especially useful in assembling received IP packet fragments.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-483">***Bandeiras de 3 bits***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-483">***3-bit flags***</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-484">Este campo contém informações de fragmentação IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-484">This field contains IP fragmentation information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-485">O bit 14 é a parte do "não se fragmentar".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-485">Bit 14 is the "don't fragment" bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-486">Se esta bit estiver definida, o datagrama ip de saída não será fragmentado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-486">If this bit is set, the outgoing IP datagram will not be fragmented.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-487">O bit 13 é a parte "mais fragmentos".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-487">Bit 13 is the "more fragments" bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-488">Se esta parte estiver definida, há mais fragmentos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-488">If this bit is set, there are more fragments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-489">Se esta parte estiver clara, este é o último fragmento do pacote IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-489">If this bit is clear, this is the last fragment of the IP packet.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-490">***Compensação de fragmentos de 13 bits***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-490">***13-bit fragment offset***</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-491">Este campo contém os 13 bits superiores da offset do fragmento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-491">This field contains the upper 13-bits of the fragment offset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-492">Por causa disso, as compensações de fragmentos só são permitidas em limites de 8 bytes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-492">Because of this, fragment offsets are only allowed on 8-byte boundaries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-493">O primeiro fragmento de um datagrama ip fragmentado terá o conjunto de bits "mais fragmentos" e terá uma compensação de 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-493">The first fragment of a fragmented IP datagram will have the "more fragments" bit set and have an offset of 0.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-494">***8 bits de tempo para viver (TTL)***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-494">***8-bit time to live (TTL)***</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-495">Este campo contém o número de routers que este datagrama pode passar, o que basicamente limita o tempo de vida útil do datagrama.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-495">This field contains the number of routers this datagram can pass, which basically limits the lifetime of the datagram.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-496">***Protocolo de 8 bits***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-496">***8-bit protocol***</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-497">Este campo especifica qual o protocolo que está a utilizar o datagrama IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-497">This field specifies which protocol is using the IP datagram.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-498">Segue-se uma lista de protocolos válidos e seus valores:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-498">The following is a list of valid protocols and their values:</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="15c79-499">- ICMP: 0x01</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-499">- ICMP: 0x01</span></span> <br /><span data-ttu-id="15c79-500">- IGMP: 0x02</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-500">- IGMP: 0x02</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="15c79-501">- TCP: 0X06</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-501">- TCP: 0X06</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="15c79-502">- UDP: 0X11</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-502">- UDP: 0X11</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-503">***Cheque de 16 bits***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-503">***16-bit checksum***</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-504">Este campo contém a parte de verificação de 16 bits que cobre apenas o cabeçalho IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-504">This field contains the 16-bit checksum that covers the IP header only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-505">Existem despesas de verificação adicionais nos protocolos de nível superior que cobrem a carga útil ip.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-505">There are additional checksums in the higher level protocols that cover the IP payload.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-506">***Endereço IP de origem de 32 bits***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-506">***32-bit source IP address***</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-507">Este campo contém o endereço IP do remetente e é sempre um endereço de anfitrião.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-507">This field contains the IP address of the sender and is always a host address.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-508">***Endereço IP de destino de 32 bits***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-508">***32-bit destination IP address***</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-509">Este campo contém o endereço IP do recetor ou dos recetores se o endereço for um endereço transmitido ou multicast.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-509">This field contains the IP address of the receiver or receivers if the address is a broadcast or multicast address.</span></span> |

### <a name="creating-ip-instances"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-510">Criação de Instâncias IP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-510">Creating IP Instances</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-511">As instâncias IP são criadas durante a inicialização ou durante o tempo de execução por fios de aplicação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-511">IP instances are created either during initialization or during runtime by application threads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-512">O endereço IPv4 inicial, máscara de rede, conjunto de pacotes predefinidos, controlador de mídia e memória e prioridade do fio IP interno são definidos pelo serviço ***nx_ip_create*** mesmo que a aplicação pretenda utilizar apenas as redes IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-512">The initial IPv4 address, network mask, default packet pool, media driver, and memory and priority of the internal IP thread are defined by the ***nx_ip_create*** service even if the application intends to use IPv6 networks only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-513">Se a aplicação rubricar a instância IP com o seu endereço IPv4 definido para um endereço inválido (0.0.0.0), presume-se que o endereço de interface será resolvido por configuração manual mais tarde, via RARP, ou através de DHCP ou protocolos semelhantes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-513">If the application initializes the IP instance with its IPv4 address set to an invalid address(0.0.0.0), it is assumed that the interface address is going to resolved by manual configuration later, via RARP, or through DHCP or similar protocols.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-514">Para sistemas com múltiplas interfaces de rede, a interface primária é designada ao chamar \***nx_ip_create** _.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-514">For systems with multiple network interfaces, the primary interface is designated when calling \***nx_ip_create** _.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-515">Cada interface adicional pode ser anexada à mesma instância IP chamando _\*_nx_ip_interface_attach_\*\*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-515">Each additional interface can be attached to the same IP instance by calling _\*_nx_ip_interface_attach_\*\*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-516">Este serviço armazena informações sobre a interface de rede (como endereço IP, máscara de rede) no bloco de controlo de interface, e associa a instância do condutor ao bloco de controlo de interface na instância IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-516">This service stores information about the network interface (such as IP address, network mask) in the interface control block, and associates the driver instance with the interface control block in the IP instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-517">Como o condutor recebe um pacote de dados, precisa de armazenar a informação da interface na estrutura NX_PACKET antes de reencaminhar para a lógica de receção IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-517">As the driver receives a data packet, it needs to store the interface information in the NX_PACKET structure before forwarding it to the IP receive logic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-518">Note que uma instância IP já deve ser criada antes de anexar quaisquer interfaces.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-518">Note an IP instance must already be created before attaching any interfaces.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-519">Os serviços IPv6 não são iniciados depois de ligar \***nx_ip_create** _.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-519">IPv6 services are not started after calling \***nx_ip_create** _.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-520">As aplicações que desejem utilizar os serviços IPv6 devem ligar para o serviço _ *_nx_ipv6_enable_*\* para iniciar o IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-520">Applications wishing to use IPv6 services must call the service _ *_nx_ipv6_enable_*\* to start IPv6.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-521">Na rede IPv6, cada interface em instância IP pode ter vários endereços globais IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-521">On the IPv6 network, each interface in an IP instance may have multiple IPv6 global addresses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-522">Além de utilizar o DHCPv6 para a atribuição de endereços IPv6, um dispositivo também pode utilizar a Configuração automática do Endereço Apátrida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-522">In addition to using DHCPv6 for IPv6 address assignment, a device may also use Stateless Address Autoconfiguration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-523">Mais informações estão disponíveis nas secções "Ip Control Block" e "Resolução de Endereços IPv6" mais tarde neste capítulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-523">More information is available in the "IP Control Block" and "IPv6 Address Resolution" sections later in this chapter.</span></span>

### <a name="ip-send"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-524">IP Enviar</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-524">IP Send</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-525">O processamento de envio IP em NetX Duo é muito simplificado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-525">The IP send processing in NetX Duo is very streamlined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-526">O ponteiro pré-final do pacote é movido para trás para acomodar o cabeçalho IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-526">The prepend pointer in the packet is moved backwards to accommodate the IP header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-527">O cabeçalho IP é preenchido (com todas as opções especificadas pela camada do protocolo de chamada), a estação de verificação IP é calculada em linha (apenas para pacotes IPv4), e o pacote é enviado para o controlador de rede associado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-527">The IP header is completed (with all the options specified by the calling protocol layer), the IP checksum is computed in-line (for IPv4 packets only), and the packet is dispatched to the associated network driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-528">Além disso, a fragmentação de saída também é coordenada a partir do processamento de envio de IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-528">In addition, outgoing fragmentation is also coordinated from within the IP send processing.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-529">Para o IPv4, a NetX Duo inicia pedidos de ARP se for necessário mapeamento físico para o endereço IP de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-529">For IPv4, NetX Duo initiates ARP requests if physical mapping is needed for the destination IP address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-530">O IPv6 usa a Neighbor Discovery para mapeamento de endereços tofísicos iPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-530">IPv6 uses Neighbor Discovery for IPv6-address-tophysical-address mapping.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-531">*Para a conectividade IPv4, os pacotes que requerem resolução de endereço IP (isto é, mapeamento físico) são encadeados na fila ARP até que o número de pacotes em fila exceda a profundidade da fila ARP (definida pelo símbolo **NX_ARP_MAX_QUEUE_DEPTH).** Se a profundidade da fila for alcançada, o NetX Duo removerá o pacote mais antigo da fila e continuará à espera da resolução de endereços para os restantes pacotes encadeados. Por outro lado, se uma entrada ARP não for resolvida, os pacotes pendentes na entrada ARP são lançados após o tempo de entrada do ARP.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-531">*For IPv4 connectivity, packets that require IP address resolution (i.e., physical mapping) are enqueued on the ARP queue until the number of packets queued exceeds the ARP queue depth (defined by the symbol **NX_ARP_MAX_QUEUE_DEPTH**). If the queue depth is reached, NetX Duo will remove the oldest packet on the queue and continue waiting for address resolution for the remaining packets enqueued. On the other hand, if an ARP entry is not resolved, the pending packets on the ARP entry are released upon ARP entry timeout.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-532">Para sistemas com múltiplas interfaces de rede, o NetX Duo escolhe uma interface baseada no endereço IP de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-532">For systems with multiple network interfaces, NetX Duo chooses an interface based on the destination IP address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-533">Aplica-se o seguinte procedimento ao processo de seleção:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-533">The following procedure applies to the selection process:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="15c79-534">Se o remetente especificar uma interface de saída e a interface for válida, utilize essa interface.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-534">If the sender specifies an outgoing interface and the interface is valid, use that interface.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="15c79-535">Se um endereço de destino for emissão IPv4 ou multicast, a primeira interface física ativada é utilizada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-535">If a destination address is IPv4 broadcast or multicast, the first enabled physical interface is used.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="15c79-536">Se o endereço de destino for encontrado na tabela de encaminhamento estático, a interface associada ao gateway é utilizada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-536">If the destination address is found in the static routing table, the interface associated with the gateway is used.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="15c79-537">Se o destino estiver ligado, a interface on-link é utilizada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-537">If the destination is on-link, the on-link interface is used.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="15c79-538">Se o endereço de destino for um endereço link-local (169.254.0.0/16), é utilizada a primeira interface válida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-538">If the destination address is a link-local address (169.254.0.0/16), the first valid interface is used.</span></span>
6. <span data-ttu-id="15c79-539">Se o gateway predefinido estiver configurado, utilize a interface associada ao gateway predefinido para transmitir o pacote.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-539">If the default gateway is configured, use the interface associated with the default gateway to transmit the packet.</span></span>
7. <span data-ttu-id="15c79-540">Finalmente, se um dos endereços IP de interface válido for o endereço link-local (169.254.0.0/16), esta interface é utilizada como endereço de origem para a transmissão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-540">Finally, if one of the valid interface IP address is link-local address (169.254.0.0/16), this interface is used as source address for the transmission.</span></span>
8. <span data-ttu-id="15c79-541">O pacote de saída é largado se tudo acima falhar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-541">The output packet is dropped if all above fails.</span></span>

### <a name="ip-receive"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-542">IP Receber</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-542">IP Receive</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-543">O processamento de receção IP é chamado do controlador de rede ou do fio IP interno (para processamento de pacotes na fila de pacotes recebidos diferidos).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-543">The IP receive processing is either called from the network driver or the internal IP thread (for processing packets on the deferred received packet queue).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-544">O processamento de receção IP examina o campo do protocolo e tenta enviar o pacote para o componente de protocolo adequado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-544">The IP receive processing examines the protocol field and attempts to dispatch the packet to the proper protocol component.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-545">Antes de o pacote ser realmente despachado, o cabeçalho IP é removido avançando o ponteiro pré-final para além do cabeçalho IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-545">Before the packet is actually dispatched, the IP header is removed by advancing the prepend pointer past the IP header.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-546">O processamento de receção IP também deteta pacotes IP fragmentados e executa as medidas necessárias para os remontar se a fragmentação estiver ativada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-546">IP receive processing also detects fragmented IP packets and performs the necessary steps to reassemble them if fragmentation is enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-547">Se for necessária fragmentação, mas não ativada, o pacote é largado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-547">If fragmentation is needed but not enabled, the packet is dropped.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-548">O NetX Duo determina a interface de rede adequada com base na interface especificada no pacote.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-548">NetX Duo determines the appropriate network interface based on the interface specified in the packet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-549">Se a interface do pacote for NU, o NetX Duo desrescumula a interface primária.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-549">If the packet interface is NULL, NetX Duo defaults to the primary interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-550">Isto é feito para garantir compatibilidade com os condutores legados NetX Duo Ethernet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-550">This is done to guarantee compatibility with legacy NetX Duo Ethernet drivers.</span></span>

### <a name="raw-ip-send"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-551">Envio de IP cru</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-551">Raw IP Send</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-552">Um pacote IP cru é um quadro IP que contém carga útil do protocolo de camada superior não suportado diretamente (e processado) por NetX Duo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-552">A raw IP packet is an IP frame that contains upper layer protocol payload not directly supported (and processed) by NetX Duo.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-553">Um pacote cru permite que os desenvolvedores definam as suas próprias aplicações baseadas em IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-553">A raw packet allows developers to define their own IP-based applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-554">Uma aplicação pode enviar pacotes IP crus diretamente utilizando o serviço ***nxd_ip_raw_packet_send** _ se o processamento de pacotes IP crus tiver sido ativado com o serviço _*_nx_ip_raw_packet_enabled._\*_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-554">An application may send raw IP packets directly using the ***nxd_ip_raw_packet_send** _ service if raw IP packet processing has been enabled with the _*_nx_ip_raw_packet_enabled_\*_ service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-555">Ao transmitir um pacote unicast numa rede IPv6, a NetX Duo determina automaticamente o melhor endereço IPv6 de origem para utilizar para enviar os pacotes, com base no endereço de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-555">When transmitting a unicast packet on an IPv6 network, NetX Duo automatically determines the best source IPv6 address to use to send the packets out on, based on the destination address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-556">Se o endereço de destino for um endereço multicast (ou transmitido para IPv4), no entanto, o NetX Duo irá por defeito na primeira interface (primária).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-556">If the destination address is a multicast (or broadcast for IPv4) address, however, NetX Duo will default to the first (primary) interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-557">Portanto, para enviar esses pacotes em interfaces secundárias, a aplicação deve utilizar o serviço _ *_nx_ip_raw_packet_source_send_*\* para especificar o endereço de origem a utilizar para o pacote de saída.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-557">Therefore, to send such packets out on secondary interfaces, the application must use the _ *_nx_ip_raw_packet_source_send_*\* service to specify the source address to use for the outgoing packet.</span></span>

### <a name="raw-ip-receive"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-558">Receber IP cru</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-558">Raw IP Receive</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-559">Se o processamento de pacotes IP cru estiver ativado, a aplicação pode receber pacotes IP crus através do serviço \***nx_ip_raw_packet_receive** _ .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-559">If raw IP packet processing is enabled, the application may receive raw IP packets through the \***nx_ip_raw_packet_receive** _ service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-560">Todos os pacotes de entrada são processados de acordo com o protocolo especificado no cabeçalho IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-560">All incoming packets are processed according to the protocol specified in the IP header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-561">Se o protocolo especificar UDP, TCP, IGMP ou ICMP, a NetX Duo processará o pacote utilizando o manipulador apropriado para o tipo de protocolo de pacote.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-561">If the protocol specifies UDP, TCP, IGMP or ICMP, NetX Duo will process the packet using the appropriate handler for the packet protocol type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-562">Se o protocolo não for um destes protocolos, e a receção ip bruta estiver ativada, o pacote de entrada será colocado na fila de pacotes brutos à espera que a aplicação o receba através do serviço _*_nx_ip_raw_packet_receive*_\* Além disso, os fios de aplicação podem suspender com um intervalo opcional enquanto aguardam um pacote IP cru. O número de pacotes que podem ser colocados na fila de pacotes brutos é limitado. O valor máximo é definido em \***NX_IP_RAW_MAX_QUEUE_DEPTH,**_ cujo valor predefinido é de 20.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-562">If the protocol is not one of these protocols, and raw IP receive is enabled, the incoming packet will be put into the raw packet queue waiting for the application to receive it via the _*_nx_ip_raw_packet_receive_*\* service. In addition, application threads may suspend with an optional timeout while waiting for a raw IP packet. The number of packets that can be queued on the raw packet queue is limited. The maximum value is defined in \***NX_IP_RAW_MAX_QUEUE_DEPTH**_, whose default value is 20.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-563">Uma aplicação pode alterar o valor máximo chamando o serviço _ *_nx_ip_raw_receive_queue_max_set_*\* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-563">An application may change the maximum value by calling the _ *_nx_ip_raw_receive_queue_max_set_*\* service.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-564">Em alternativa, a biblioteca NetX Duo pode ser construída com \***NX_ENABLE_IP_RAW_PACKET_FILTER\*.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-564">Alternatively, the NetX Duo library may be built with \***NX_ENABLE_IP_RAW_PACKET_FILTER\*.**</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-565">Neste modo de funcionamento, a aplicação fornece uma função de retorno que é invocada sempre que um pacote com um tipo de protocolo não manipulado é recebido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-565">In this mode of operation, the application provides a callback function that is invoked every time a packet with an unhandled protocol type is received.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-566">A lógica de receção IP encaminha o pacote para o pacote cru definido pelo utilizador receber a rotina do filtro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-566">The IP receive logic forwards the packet to the user-defined raw packet receive filter routine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-567">A rotina do filtro decide se mantém ou não o pacote cru para o processo futuro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-567">The filter routine decides whether or not to keep the raw packet for future process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-568">O valor de retorno da rotina de retorno indica se o pacote foi processado pelo filtro de receção de pacote cru.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-568">The return value from the callback routine indicates whether the packet has been processed by the raw packet receive filter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-569">Se o pacote for processado pela função de retorno, o pacote deve ser libertado após a aplicação ser feita com o pacote.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-569">If the packet is processed by the callback function, the packet should be released after the application is done with the packet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-570">Caso contrário, a NetX Duo é responsável pela libertação do pacote.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-570">Otherwise, NetX Duo is responsible for releasing the packet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-571">Consulte a **_nx_ip_raw_packet_filter_set_** para obter mais informações sobre como utilizar a função de filtro de pacotes brutos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-571">Refer to the **_nx_ip_raw_packet_filter_set_** for more information on how to use the raw packet filter function.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-572">\*A função de invólucro BSD para NetX Duo baseia-se na função de filtro de pacotes brutos para manusear tomadas em bruto BSD.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-572">\*The BSD wrapper function for NetX Duo relies on the raw packet filter function to handle BSD raw sockets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-573">Por isso, para suportar a tomada em bruto no invólucro BSD, a biblioteca NetX Duo deve ser construída com ***NX_ENABLE_IP_RAW_PACKET_FILTER** _ definido, e a aplicação não deve usar o _*_nx_ip_raw_packet_filter_set_\*_ para instalar o seu próprio filtro de pacote cru functions._</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-573">Therefore, to support raw socket in the BSD wrapper, the NetX Duo library must be built with ***NX_ENABLE_IP_RAW_PACKET_FILTER** _ defined, and the application should not use the _*_nx_ip_raw_packet_filter_set_\*_ to install its own raw packet filter functions._</span></span>

### <a name="default-packet-pool"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-574">Piscina de pacotes predefinidos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-574">Default Packet Pool</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-575">Cada instância IP recebe um pacote de pacote padrão durante a criação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-575">Each IP instance is given a default packet pool during creation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-576">Esta piscina de pacotes é usada para alocar pacotes para ARP, RARP, ICMP, IGMP, vários pacotes de controlo TCP (SYN, ACK, e assim por diante), Neighbor Discovery, Router Discovery e Duplicate Address Detection.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-576">This packet pool is used to allocate packets for ARP, RARP, ICMP, IGMP, various TCP control packets (SYN, ACK, and so on), Neighbor Discovery, Router Discovery, and Duplicate Address Detection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-577">Se o pacote predefinido estiver vazio quando o NetX Duo precisar de alocar um pacote, o NetX Duo poderá ter de abortar a operação em particular e devolverá uma mensagem de erro se possível.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-577">If the default packet pool is empty when NetX Duo needs to allocate a packet, NetX Duo may have to abort the particular operation, and will return an error message if possible.</span></span>

### <a name="ip-helper-thread"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-578">Fio de ajudante IP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-578">IP Helper Thread</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-579">Cada instância IP tem um fio de ajuda.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-579">Each IP instance has a helper thread.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-580">Este fio é responsável pelo manuseamento de todo o processamento de pacotes diferidos e de todo o processamento periódico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-580">This thread is responsible for handling all deferred packet processing and all periodic processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-581">O fio do ajudante IP é criado em ***nx_ip_create.*** É aqui que o fio é dado a sua pilha e prioridade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-581">The IP helper thread is created in ***nx_ip_create.*** This is where the thread is given its stack and priority.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-582">Note que o primeiro processamento na linha de ajuda IP é terminar a inicialização do controlador de rede associada ao serviço de criação IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-582">Note that the first processing in the IP helper thread is to finish the network driver initialization associated with the IP create service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-583">Após a inicialização do controlador de rede estar concluída, o fio do ajudante inicia um ciclo interminável para processar pacotes e pedidos periódicos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-583">After the network driver initialization is complete, the helper thread starts an endless loop to process packet and periodic requests.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-584">*Se o comportamento inexplicável for visto dentro do fio do ajudante IP, aumentar o tamanho da pilha durante o serviço de criação IP é o primeiro passo de depurar. Se a pilha for muito pequena, o fio do ajudante IP pode estar a sobrepor-se à memória, o que pode causar problemas incomuns.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-584">*If unexplained behavior is seen within the IP helper thread, increasing its stack size during the IP create service is the first debugging step. If the stack is too small, the IP helper thread could possibly be overwriting memory, which may cause unusual problems.*</span></span>

### <a name="thread-suspension"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-585">Suspensão do fio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-585">Thread Suspension</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-586">Os fios de aplicação podem suspender enquanto tentam receber pacotes IP crus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-586">Application threads can suspend while attempting to receive raw IP packets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-587">Depois de recebido um pacote cru, o novo pacote é dado ao primeiro fio suspenso e esse fio é retomado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-587">After a raw packet is received, the new packet is given to the first thread suspended and that thread is resumed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-588">Os serviços da NetX Duo para receber pacotes têm um tempo de suspensão opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-588">NetX Duo services for receiving packets all have an optional suspension timeout.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-589">Quando um pacote é recebido ou o tempo limite expira, o fio de aplicação é retomado com o estado de conclusão adequado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-589">When a packet is received or the timeout expires, the application thread is resumed with the appropriate completion status.</span></span>

### <a name="ip-statistics-and-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-590">Estatísticas e erros ip</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-590">IP Statistics and Errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-591">Se ativado, o Duo NetX regista várias estatísticas e erros que podem ser úteis à aplicação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-591">If enabled, the NetX Duo keeps track of several statistics and errors that may be useful to the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-592">As seguintes estatísticas e relatórios de erro são mantidos para cada instância DEP:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-592">The following statistics and error reports are maintained for each IP instance:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-593">Total de pacotes IP enviados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-593">Total IP Packets Sent</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-594">Total de bytes IP enviados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-594">Total IP Bytes Sent</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-595">Total de pacotes IP recebidos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-595">Total IP Packets Received</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-596">Total de bytes IP recebidos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-596">Total IP Bytes Received</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-597">Total de pacotes inválidos IP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-597">Total IP Invalid Packets</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-598">Total de pacotes de receção IP abandonados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-598">Total IP Receive Packets Dropped</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-599">Total IP Receber Erros de Checkum</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-599">Total IP Receive Checksum Errors</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-600">Total IP Enviar Pacotes Abandonados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-600">Total IP Send Packets Dropped</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-601">Total de fragmentos ip enviados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-601">Total IP Fragments Sent</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-602">Total de fragmentos ip recebidos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-602">Total IP Fragments Received</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-603">Todas estas estatísticas e relatórios de erro estão disponíveis para a aplicação com o serviço ***nx_ip_info_get.***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-603">All of these statistics and error reports are available to the application with the ***nx_ip_info_get*** service.</span></span>

### <a name="ip-control-block-nx_ip"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-604">NX_IP do Bloco de Controlo IP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-604">IP Control Block NX_IP</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-605">As características de cada instância IP encontram-se no seu bloco de controlo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-605">The characteristics of each IP instance are found in its control block.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-606">Contém informações úteis, tais como endereços IP e máscaras de rede de cada dispositivo de rede, e uma tabela de IP vizinho e mapeamento de endereços de hardware físico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-606">It contains useful information such as the IP addresses and network masks of each network device, and a table of neighbor IP and physical hardware address mapping.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-607">Esta estrutura é definida na _file \***nx_api.h.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-607">This structure is defined in the \***nx_api.h** _file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-608">Se o IPv6 estiver ativado, também contém um conjunto de endereços IPv6, número dos quais é especificado pela opção configurável do utilizador _\*_NX_MAX_IPV6_ADDRESSES_\*\*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-608">If IPv6 is enabled, it also contains an array of IPv6 address, the number of which is specified by the user configurable option _\*_NX_MAX_IPV6_ADDRESSES_\*\*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-609">O valor predefinido permite que cada interface de rede física tenha três endereços IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-609">The default value allows each physical network interface to have three IPv6 addresses.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-610">Os blocos de controlo de instância IP podem ser localizados em qualquer lugar da memória, mas é mais comum fazer do bloco de controlo uma estrutura global definindo-o fora do âmbito de qualquer função.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-610">IP instance control blocks can be located anywhere in memory, but it is most common to make the control block a global structure by defining it outside the scope of any function.</span></span>

### <a name="static-ipv4-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-611">Encaminhamento estático IPv4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-611">Static IPv4 Routing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-612">A funcionalidade de encaminhamento estático permite que uma aplicação especifique uma rede IPv4 e o próximo endereço de lúpulo para endereços IP específicos fora da rede.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-612">The static routing feature allows an application to specify an IPv4 network and next hop address for specific out of network destination IP addresses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-613">Se o encaminhamento estático estiver ativado, o NetX Duo procura através da tabela de encaminhamento estático para uma entrada correspondente ao endereço de destino do pacote a enviar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-613">If static routing is enabled, NetX Duo searches through the static routing table for an entry matching the destination address of the packet to send.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-614">Se não for encontrado qualquer correspondência, o NetX Duo procura através da lista de interfaces físicas e escolhe um endereço IP de origem e próximo endereço de lúpulo baseado no endereço IP de destino e na máscara de rede.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-614">If no match is found, NetX Duo searches through the list of physical interfaces and chooses a source IP address and next hop address based on the destination IP address and the network mask.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-615">Se o destino não corresponder a nenhum dos endereços IP dos controladores de rede ligados à instância IP, o NetX Duo escolhe uma interface que está diretamente ligada ao gateway predefinido e utiliza o endereço IP da interface como endereço de origem, e o gateway predefinido como o próximo salto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-615">If the destination does not match any of the IP addresses of the network drivers attached to the IP instance, NetX Duo chooses an interface that is directly connected to the default gateway, and uses the IP address of the interface as source address, and the default gateway as the next hop.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-616">As entradas podem ser adicionadas e removidas da tabela de encaminhamento estático utilizando os serviços ***nx_ip_static_route_add** _ e _ *_nx_ip_static_route_delete_** respectivamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-616">Entries can be added and removed from the static routing table using the ***nx_ip_static_route_add** _ and _ *_nx_ip_static_route_delete_** services, respectively.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-617">Para utilizar o encaminhamento estático, a aplicação do anfitrião deve ativar esta função definindo ***NX_ENABLE_IP_STATIC_ROUTING.***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-617">To use static routing, the host application must enable this feature by defining ***NX_ENABLE_IP_STATIC_ROUTING.***</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-618">*Ao adicionar uma entrada na tabela de encaminhamento estático, o NetX Duo verifica uma entrada correspondente para o endereço de destino especificado já na tabela. Se existir, dá preferência à entrada com a rede mais pequena (prefixo mais longo) na máscara de rede.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-618">*When adding an entry to the static routing table, NetX Duo checks for a matching entry for the specified destination address already in the table. If one exists, it gives preference to the entry with the smaller network (longer prefix) in the network mask.*</span></span>

### <a name="ipv4-forwarding"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-619">Encaminhamento IPv4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-619">IPv4 Forwarding</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-620">Se o pacote IPv4 de entrada não estiver destinado a este nó e a função de reencaminhamento IPv4 estiver ativada, a NetX Duo tenta encaminhar o pacote através das outras interfaces.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-620">If the incoming IPv4 packet is not destined for this node and IPv4 forwarding feature is enabled, NetX Duo attempts to forward the packet out via the other interfaces.</span></span>  

### <a name="ip-fragmentation"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-621">Fragmentação ip</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-621">IP Fragmentation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-622">O dispositivo de rede pode ter limites no tamanho dos pacotes de saída.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-622">The network device may have limits on the size of outgoing packets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-623">Este limite é chamado de unidade de transmissão máxima (MTU).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-623">This limit is called the maximum transmission unit (MTU).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-624">IP MTU é o maior tamanho de quadro IP que o controlador de camada de ligação é capaz de transmitir sem fragmentar o pacote IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-624">IP MTU is the largest IP frame size a link layer driver is able to transmit without fragmenting the IP packet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-625">Durante uma fase de inicialização do controlador do dispositivo, o módulo do condutor deve configurar o seu tamanho IP MTU através do ***serviço nx_ip_interface_mtu_set.***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-625">During a device driver initialization phase, the driver module must configure its IP MTU size via the service ***nx_ip_interface_mtu_set.***</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-626">Embora não recomendado, a aplicação pode gerar datagramas maiores do que o IP MTU subjacente suportado pelo dispositivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-626">Although not recommended, the application may generate datagrams larger than the underlying IP MTU supported by the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-627">Antes de transmitir tais datagramas de IP, a camada IP deve fragmentar estes pacotes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-627">Before transmitting such IP datagram, the IP layer must fragment these packets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-628">Ao receber quadros IP fragmentados, a extremidade recetora deve armazenar todos os quadros IP fragmentados com o mesmo ID de fragmentação e montá-los em ordem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-628">On receiving fragmented IP frames, the receiving end must store all fragmented IP frames with the same fragmentation ID, and reassemble them in order.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-629">Se a lógica de receção ip não for capaz de recolher todos os fragmentos para restaurar o quadro IP original no tempo, todos os fragmentos são libertados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-629">If the IP receive logic is unable to collect all the fragments to restore the original IP frame in time, all the fragments are released.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-630">Cabe ao protocolo da camada superior detetar tal perda de pacote e recuperá-la.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-630">It is up to the upper layer protocol to detect such packet loss and recover from it.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-631">A fragmentação do IP aplica-se tanto aos pacotes IPv4 como IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-631">The IP fragmentation applies to both IPv4 and IPv6 packets.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-632">Para suportar a fragmentação e o funcionamento da fragmentação IP, o designer de sistema deve ativar a função de fragmentação IP no NetX Duo utilizando o serviço ***nx_ip_fragment_enable.***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-632">In order to support IP fragmentation and reassembly operation, the system designer must enable the IP fragmentation feature in NetX Duo using the ***nx_ip_fragment_enable*** service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-633">Se esta função não estiver ativada, os pacotes IP fragmentados de entrada são descartados, bem como pacotes que excedam o MTU do controlador de rede.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-633">If this feature is not enabled, incoming fragmented IP packets are discarded, as well as packets that exceed the network driver's MTU.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-634">\*A lógica de fragmentação IP pode ser completamente removida definindo \***NX_DISABLE_FRAGMENTATION** _ ao construir a biblioteca NetX Duo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-634">\*The IP Fragmentation logic can be removed completely by defining \***NX_DISABLE_FRAGMENTATION** _ when building the NetX Duo library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-635">Ao fazê-lo, ajuda a reduzir o tamanho do código do NetX Duo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-635">Doing so helps reduce the code size of NetX Duo.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-636">Note que, nesta situação, as funções de fragmentação/remontagem do IPv4 e do IPv6 são disabled._</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-636">Note that in this situation, both the IPv4 and IPv6 fragmentation/reassembly functions are disabled._</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-637">*Se **NX_DISABLE_CHAINED_PACKET** estiver definido, a fragmentação ip deve ser desativada.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-637">*If **NX_DISABLE_CHAINED_PACKET** is defined, IP fragmentation must be disabled.*</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-638">*Numa rede IPv6, os routers não fragmentam um datagrama se o tamanho do datagrama exceder o seu tamanho mínimo de MTU. Por conseguinte, cabe ao dispositivo de envio determinar o mínimo MTU entre a fonte e o destino, e garantir que o tamanho do datagrama IP não exceda o caminho MTU. No NetX Duo, a descoberta IPv6 PATH MTU pode ser ativada através da construção da biblioteca NetX Duo com o símbolo **NX_ENABLE_IPV6_PATH_MTU_DISCOVERY** definido.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-638">*In an IPv6 network, routers do not fragment a datagram if the size of the datagram exceeds its minimum MTU size. Therefore, it is up to the sending device to determine the minimum MTU between the source and the destination, and to ensure the IP datagram size does not exceed the path MTU. In NetX Duo, IPv6 PATH MTU discovery can be enabled by building NetX Duo library with the symbol **NX_ENABLE_IPV6_PATH_MTU_DISCOVERY** defined.*</span></span>

## <a name="address-resolution-protocol-arp-in-ipv4"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-639">Protocolo de Resolução de Endereços (ARP) no IPv4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-639">Address Resolution Protocol (ARP) in IPv4</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-640">O Protocolo de Resolução de Endereços (ARP) é responsável por mapear dinamicamente endereços IPv4 de 32 bits aos dos meios físicos subjacentes (RFC 826).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-640">The Address Resolution Protocol (ARP) is responsible for dynamically mapping 32-bit IPv4 addresses to those of the underlying physical media (RFC 826).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-641">Ethernet é o meio físico mais típico, e suporta endereços de 48 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-641">Ethernet is the most typical physical media, and it supports 48-bit addresses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-642">A necessidade de ARP é determinada pelo controlador de rede fornecido ao serviço \***nx_ip_create** _ .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-642">The need for ARP is determined by the network driver supplied to the \***nx_ip_create** _ service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-643">Se for necessário um mapeamento físico, o controlador de rede deve utilizar o serviço _ *_nx_interface_address_mapping_needed_*\* para configurar corretamente a interface do controlador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-643">If physical mapping is required, the network driver must use the _ *_nx_interface_address_mapping_needed_*\* service to configure the driver interface properly.</span></span>

### <a name="arp-enable"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-644">Ativar a ARP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-644">ARP Enable</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-645">Para que a ARP funcione corretamente, deve primeiro ser ativada pela aplicação com o serviço ***nx_arp_enable.***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-645">For ARP to function properly, it must first be enabled by the application with the ***nx_arp_enable*** service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-646">Este serviço estabelece várias estruturas de dados para o processamento de ARP, incluindo a criação de uma área de cache ARP a partir da memória fornecida ao serviço de ativação ARP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-646">This service sets up various data structures for ARP processing, including the creation of an ARP cache area from the memory supplied to the ARP enable service.</span></span>

### <a name="arp-cache"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-647">ARP Cache</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-647">ARP Cache</span></span>
