<span data-ttu-id="15c79-932">No exemplo acima, se o endereço MAC da interface for 54:32:10:1A:BC:67, o endereço local de ligação correspondente seria:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-932">In the example above, if the MAC address of the interface is 54:32:10:1A:BC:67, the corresponding link-local address would be:</span></span>

```c
FE80::5632:10FF:FE1A:BC67
```
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-933">Note que a parte de ID do anfitrião do endereço IPv6 **(5632:10FF:FE1A:BC67)** é composta pelo endereço MAC de 6 bytes, com as seguintes modificações:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-933">Note that the host ID portion of the IPv6 address (**5632:10FF:FE1A:BC67**) is made up of the 6-byte MAC address, with the following modifications:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-934">**0xFFFE** inseridas entre byte 3 e byte 4 do endereço MAC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-934">**0xFFFE** inserted between byte 3 and byte 4 of the MAC address</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-935">A segunda parte mais baixa do primeiro byte do endereço MAC (bit U/L) está definida para 1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-935">Second lowest bit of the first byte of the MAC address (U/L bit) is set to 1</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-936">Consulte o RFC 2464 (Transmissão de Pacotes IPv6 através da Rede Ethernet) para obter mais informações sobre como construir a parte hospedeira de um endereço IPv6 a partir do seu endereço MAC de interface.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-936">Refer to RFC 2464 (Transmission of IPv6 Packets over Ethernet Network) for more information on how to construct the host portion of an IPv6 address from its interface MAC address.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-937">Existem alguns endereços multicast especiais para o envio de mensagens multicast para um ou mais anfitriões no IPv6:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-937">There are a few special multicast addresses for sending multicast messages to one or more hosts in IPv6:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="15c79-938">Group</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-938">Group</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="15c79-939">Endereço</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-939">Address</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="15c79-940">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-940">Description</span></span>  |
|---|---|---|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-941">Todos os grupos de nós</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-941">All nodes group</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-942">**FF02::1**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-942">**FF02::1**</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-943">Todos os anfitriões da rede local</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-943">All hosts on the local network</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-944">Todos os routers grupo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-944">All routers group</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-945">**FF02::2**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-945">**FF02::2**</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-946">Todos os routers da rede local</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-946">All routers on the local network</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-947">Nó solicitado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-947">Solicited-node</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-948">**FF02::1:FF00:0/104**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-948">**FF02::1:FF00:0/104**</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-949">Explicado abaixo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-949">Explained below</span></span>|

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-950">Um endereço multicast de nó solicitado visa anfitriões específicos na ligação local em vez de todos os anfitriões IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-950">A solicited-node multicast address targets specific hosts on the local link rather than all the IPv6 hosts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-951">Consiste no prefixo **FF02::1:FF00:0/104,** que é de 104 bits e os últimos 24 bits do endereço IPv6 alvo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-951">It consists of the prefix **FF02::1:FF00:0/104**, which is 104 bits and the last 24-bits of the target IPv6 address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-952">Por exemplo, um endereço IPv6 **205B:209D:D028::F058:D1C8:1024** tem um endereço multicast solicitado de endereço **FF02::1:FFC8:1024**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-952">For example, an IPv6 address **205B:209D:D028::F058:D1C8:1024** has a solicitednode multicast address of address **FF02::1:FFC8:1024**.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-953">*A notação do cólon duplo indica que os pedaços de intervenção são todos zeros. **FF02::1:FF00:0/104** totalmente expandido parece* **FF02:0000:0000:0000:000:0001:FF00:000:000:000**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-953">*The double colon notation indicates the intervening bits are all zeroes. **FF02::1:FF00:0/104** fully expanded looks like* **FF02:0000:0000:0000:0000:0001:FF00:0000**</span></span>

### <a name="global-addresses"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-954">Endereços Globais</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-954">Global Addresses</span></span>    
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-955">Um exemplo de um endereço global IPv6 é **2001:0123:4567:89AB:CDEF::1** NetX Duo armazena endereços IPv6 na estrutura NXD_ADDRESS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-955">An example of an IPv6 global address is **2001:0123:4567:89AB:CDEF::1** NetX Duo stores IPv6 addresses in the NXD_ADDRESS structure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-956">No exemplo abaixo, a variável NXD_ADDRESS **global_ipv6_address** contém um endereço IPv6 unicast.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-956">In the example below, the NXD_ADDRESS variable **global_ipv6_address** contains a unicast IPv6 address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-957">O exemplo a seguir demonstra que um dispositivo NetX Duo cria um endereço global IPv6 específico para o seu dispositivo primário:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-957">The following example demonstrates a NetX Duo device creating a specific IPv6 global address for its primary device:</span></span>

```c
NXD_ADDRESS global_ipv6_address;
UINT        primary_interface_index = 0;

global_ipv6_address.nxd_ip_version = NX_IP_VERSION_V6;
global_ipv6_address.nxd_ip_address.v6[0] = 0x20010123;
global_ipv6_address.nxd_ip_address.v6[1] = 0x456789AB;
global_ipv6_address.nxd_ip_address.v6[2] = 0xCDEF0000;
global_ipv6_address.nxd_ip_address.v6[3] = 0x00000001;

status = nxd_ipv6_address_set(
            &ip_0,
            primary_interface_index,
            &global_ipv6_address,
            64,
            NX_NULL);
```
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-958">Note que o prefixo deste endereço IPv6 é **2001:0123:4567:89AB**, que tem 64 bits de comprimento e é um comprimento prefixo comum para endereços IPv6 unicast global no Ethernet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-958">Note that the prefix of this IPv6 address is **2001:0123:4567:89AB**, which is 64 bits long and is a common prefix length for global unicast IPv6 addresses on Ethernet.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-959">A estrutura NXD_ADDRESS também possui endereços IPv4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-959">The NXD_ADDRESS structure also holds IPv4 addresses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-960">Um endereço IP de **192.1.168.10** **(0xC001A80A)** armazenado em global_ipv4_address teria o seguinte layout de memória:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-960">An IP address of **192.1.168.10** (**0xC001A80A**) stored in global_ipv4_address would have the following memory layout:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-961">Campo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-961">Field</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-962">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-962">Value</span></span> |
|---|---|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-963">versão global_ipv4_address.nxd_ip_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-963">global_ipv4_address.nxd_ip_version</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-964">NX_IP_VERSION_V4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-964">NX_IP_VERSION_V4</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-965">global_ipv4_address.nxd_ip_address.v4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-965">global_ipv4_address.nxd_ip_address.v4</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-966">0xC001A80A</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-966">0xC001A80A</span></span>|

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-967">Quando uma aplicação passa um endereço para os serviços NetX Duo, o campo *nxd_ip_version* deve especificar a versão IP correta para o manuseamento adequado do pacote.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-967">When an application passes an address to NetX Duo services, the *nxd_ip_version* field must specify the correct IP version for proper packet handling.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-968">Para ser retrocompatível com as aplicações NetX existentes, a NetX Duo suporta todos os serviços NetX.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-968">To be backward compatible with existing NetX applications, NetX Duo supports all NetX services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-969">Internamente, o NetX Duo converte o tipo de endereço IPv4 ULONG para um tipo de dados NXD_ADDRESS antes de reencaminho para o serviço NetX Duo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-969">Internally, NetX Duo converts the IPv4 address type ULONG to an NXD_ADDRESS data type before forwarding it to the actual NetX Duo service.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-970">O exemplo a seguir ilustra a semelhança e as diferenças entre serviços na NetX e netX Duo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-970">The following example illustrates the similarity and the differences between services in NetX and NetX Duo.</span></span>

```c
/* Make a connection to the destination IPv4 address
   192.1.168.12 through an already created TCP socket bound
   to the well known HTTP port number 80. */

global_ipv4_address.nxd_ip_version = NX_IP_VERSION_V4;
global_ipv4_address.nxd_ip_address.v4 = 0xC001A80C;

nxd_tcp_client_socket_connect(&tcp_socket,
                              &global_ipv4_address,
                              port_number,
                              NX_WAIT_FOREVER);
```

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-971">Segue-se a API líquida equivalente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-971">The following is the equivalent NetX API:</span></span>

```c
ULONG         server_ip = 0xC001A80C;
NX_TCP_SOCKET tcp_socket;
UINT          port_number = 80;

nx_tcp_client_socket_connect(&tcp_socket,
                             server_ip,
                             port_number,
                             NX_WAIT_FOREVER); 
```

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-972">*Os desenvolvedores de aplicações são encorajados a usar a versão nxd destes APIs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-972">*Application developers are encouraged to use the nxd version of these APIs*.</span></span>

### <a name="ipv6-default-routers"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-973">Routers padrão IPv6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-973">IPv6 Default Routers</span></span>    
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-974">O IPv6 usa um router predefinido para encaminhar pacotes para destinos offlink.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-974">IPv6 uses a default router to forward packets to offlink destinations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-975">O serviço NetX Duo ***nxd_ipv6_default_router_add*** permite que uma aplicação adicione um router IPv6 à tabela de routers predefinido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-975">The NetX Duo service ***nxd_ipv6_default_router_add*** enables an application to add an IPv6 router to the default router table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-976">Consulte o capítulo 4 "Descrição dos Serviços" para serviços de router mais predefinidos oferecidos pela NetX Duo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-976">See Chapter 4 "Description of Services" for more default router services offered by NetX Duo.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-977">Ao encaminhar os pacotes IPv6, o NetX Duo verifica primeiro se o destino do pacote está ligado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-977">When forwarding IPv6 packets, NetX Duo first checks if the packet destination is on-link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-978">Caso contrário, o NetX Duo verifica a tabela de encaminhamento predefinido para um router válido para encaminhar o pacote off-link para.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-978">If not, NetX Duo checks the default routing table for a valid router to forward the off-link packet to.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-979">Para remover um router da tabela de routers predefinido IPv6, a aplicação deve utilizar o serviço \***nxd_ipv6_default_router_delete** _.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-979">To remove a router from the IPv6 default router table, application shall use the service \***nxd_ipv6_default_router_delete** _.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-980">Para obter entradas da tabela de routers predefinido IPv6, utilize o serviço _\*_nxd_ipv6_default_router_entry_get_\*\*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-980">To obtain entries of the IPv6 default router table, use the service _\*_nxd_ipv6_default_router_entry_get_\*\*.</span></span>

### <a name="ipv6-header"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-981">Cabeçalho IPv6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-981">IPv6 Header</span></span>    
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-982">O cabeçalho IPv6 foi modificado a partir do cabeçalho IPv4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-982">The IPv6 header has been modified from the IPv4 header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-983">Ao atribuir um pacote, o chamador especifica o protocolo de aplicação (por exemplo, UDP, TCP), tamanho tampão em bytes e limite de lúpulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-983">When allocating a packet, the caller specifies the application protocol (e.g., UDP, TCP), buffer size in bytes, and hop limit.</span></span>   

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-984">A figura 9 mostra o formato do cabeçalho IPv6 e a tabela lista os componentes do cabeçalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-984">Figure 9 shows the format of the IPv6 header and the table lists the header components.</span></span>

![Diagrama do formato do cabeçalho IPv6.](./media/user-guide/image18.png)

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-986">**FIGURA 9. Formato iPv6 Header**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-986">**FIGURE 9. IPv6 Header Format**</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-987">Cabeçalho IP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-987">IP header</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="15c79-988">Objetivo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-988">Purpose</span></span> |
|---|---|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-989">Versão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-989">Version</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-990">Campo de 4 bits para a versão IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-990">4-bit field for IP version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-991">Para as redes IPv6, o valor neste campo deve ser de 6; Para as redes IPv4 deve ser 4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-991">For IPv6 networks, the value in this field must be 6; For IPv4 networks it must be 4.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-992">Classe de Tráfego</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-992">Traffic Class</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-993">Campo de 8 bits que armazena a informação da classe de tráfego.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-993">8-bit field that stores the traffic class information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-994">Este campo não é utilizado pela NetX Duo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-994">This field is not used by NetX Duo.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-995">Rótulo de fluxo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-995">Flow Label</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-996">Campo de 20 bits para identificar exclusivamente o fluxo, se houver, com o qual um pacote está associado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-996">20-bit field to uniquely identify the flow, if any, that a packet is associated with.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-997">Um valor de zero indica que o pacote não pertence a um fluxo específico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-997">A value of zero indicates the packet does not belong to a particular flow.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-998">Este campo substitui o campo *TOS* no IPv4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-998">This field replaces the *TOS* field in IPv4.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-999">Comprimento da carga útil</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-999">Payload Length</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1000">Campo de 16 bits indicando a quantidade de dados nos bytes do pacote IPv6 após o cabeçalho de base IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1000">16-bit field indicating the amount of data in bytes of the IPv6 packet following the IPv6 base header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1001">Isto inclui todos os cabeçalhos e dados do protocolo encapsulados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1001">This includes all encapsulated protocol header and data.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1002">Próximo Cabeçalho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1002">Next Header</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1003">Campo de 8 bits indicando o tipo do cabeçalho de extensão que segue o cabeçalho base IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1003">8-bit field indicating the type of the extension header that follows the IPv6 base header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1004">Este campo substitui o campo *Protocolo* no IPv4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1004">This field replaces the *Protocol* field in IPv4.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1005">Limite de lúpulo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1005">Hop Limit</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1006">Campo de 8 bits que limita o número de routers que o pacote é permitido passar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1006">8-bit field that limits the number of routers the packet is allowed to go through.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1007">Este campo substitui o campo *TTL* no IPv4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1007">This field replaces the *TTL* field in IPv4.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1008">Endereço de Origem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1008">Source Address</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1009">Campo de 128 bits que armazena o endereço IPv6 do remetente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1009">128-bit field that stores the IPv6 address of the sender.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1010">Endereço de destino</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1010">Destination Address</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1011">Campo de 128 bits que faz nerv6 do destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1011">128-bit field that sores the IPv6 address of the destination.</span></span>|

### <a name="enabling-ipv6-in-netx-duo"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1012">Ativar o IPv6 em NetX Duo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1012">Enabling IPv6 in NetX Duo</span></span>    
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1013">Por padrão, o IPv6 está ativado no NetX Duo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1013">By default IPv6 is enabled in NetX Duo.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1014">Os serviços IPv6 estão ativados no NetX Duo se a opção configurável ***NX_DISABLE_IPV6** _ em _nx_user.h* não estiver definida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1014">IPv6 services are enabled in NetX Duo if the configurable option ***NX_DISABLE_IPV6** _ in _nx_user.h* is not defined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1015">Se ***NX_DISABLE_IPV6*** estiver definido, o NetX Duo apenas oferecerá serviços IPv4, e todos os módulos e serviços relacionados com o IPv6 não estão integrados na biblioteca NetX Duo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1015">If ***NX_DISABLE_IPV6*** is defined, NetX Duo will only offer IPv4 services, and all the IPv6-related modules and services are not built into NetX Duo library.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1016">O seguinte serviço é fornecido para aplicações para configurar o endereço IPv6 do dispositivo: ***nxd_ipv6_address_set***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1016">The following service is provided for applications to configure the device IPv6 address: ***nxd_ipv6_address_set***</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1017">Além de configurar manualmente os endereços IPv6 do dispositivo, o sistema também pode utilizar a Configuração Automática de Endereços Apátridas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1017">In addition to manually setting the device's IPv6 addresses, the system may also use Stateless Address Autoconfiguration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1018">Para utilizar esta opção, a aplicação deve ligar \***nxd_ipv6_enable** _ para iniciar os serviços IPv6 no dispositivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1018">To use this option, the application must call \***nxd_ipv6_enable** _ to start IPv6 services on the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1019">Além disso, os serviços ICMPv6 devem ser iniciados ligando para _*_nxd_icmp_enable,_*_ o que permite à NetX Duo realizar serviços como Solicitação router, Neighbor Discovery e Duplicate Address Detection.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1019">In addition, ICMPv6 services must be started by calling _*_nxd_icmp_enable_*_, which enables NetX Duo to perform services such as Router Solicitation, Neighbor Discovery, and Duplicate Address Detection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1020">Note que _*_nx_icmp_enable_*_ só inicia o ICMP para os serviços IPv4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1020">Note that _*_nx_icmp_enable_*_ only starts ICMP for IPv4 services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1021">_*_nxd_icmp_enable_*_ inicia serviços ICMP tanto para iPv4 como IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1021">_*_nxd_icmp_enable_*_ starts ICMP services for both IPv4 and IPv6.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1022">Se o sistema não necessitar de serviços ICMPv6, então _ *_nx_icmp_enable_*\* pode ser utilizado para que o módulo ICMPv6 não esteja ligado ao sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1022">If the system does not need ICMPv6 services, then _ *_nx_icmp_enable_*\* can be used so the ICMPv6 module is not linked into the system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1023">O exemplo a seguir mostra um procedimento típico de inicialização NetX Duo IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1023">The following example shows a typical NetX Duo IPv6 initialization procedure.</span></span>

```c
/* Assume ip_0 has been created and IPv4 services (such as ARP,
   ICMP, have been enabled. */
#define SECONDARY_INTERFACE 1

/* Enable IPv6 */
status = nxd_ipv6_enable(&ip_0);

if(status != NX_SUCCESS)
{
    /* nxd_ipv6_enable failed. */
}

/* Enable ICMPv6 */
status = nxd_icmp_enable(&ip_0);
if(status != NX_SUCCESS)
{
    /* nxd_icmp_enable failed. */
}

/* Configure the link local address on the primary interface. */
status = nxd_ipv6_address_set(&ip_0, 0, NX_NULL, 10, NX_NULL);

/* Configure ip_0 primary interface global address. */
ip_address.nxd_ip_version = NX_IP_VERSION_V6
ip_address.nxd_ip_address.v6[0] = 0x20010db8;
ip_address.nxd_ip_address.v6[1] = 0x0000f101;
ip_address.nxd_ip_address.v6[2] = 0;
ip_address.nxd_ip_address.v6[3] = 0x202;

/* Configure global address of the primary interface. */
status = nxd_ipv6_address_set(&ip_0, SECONDARY_INTERFACE,
                              &ip_address, 64, NX_NULL);
```                              

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1024">Os protocolos de camada superior (como TCP e UDP) podem ser ativados antes ou depois do início do IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1024">Upper layer protocols (such as TCP and UDP) can be enabled either before or after IPv6 starts.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]  
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1025">*Os serviços IPv6 só estão disponíveis após a inicialção do fio IP e o dispositivo está ativado.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1025">*IPv6 services are available only after IP thread is initialized and the device is enabled.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1026">Depois de a interface estar ativada (ou seja, o controlador do dispositivo de interface está pronto para enviar e receber dados, e foi obtido um endereço local de ligação válido), o dispositivo poderá obter endereços IPv6 globais por um destes métodos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1026">After the interface is enabled (i.e.,the interface device driver is ready to send and receive data, and a valid link local address has been obtained), the device may obtain global IPv6 addresses by one of the these methods:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1027">Configuração de auto endereço apátrida;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1027">Stateless Address Auto Configuration;</span></span>  
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1028">Configuração manual do endereço IPv6;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1028">Manual IPv6 address configuration;</span></span>  
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1029">Configuração de endereço via DHCPv6 (com pacote opcional DHCPv6)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1029">Address configuration via DHCPv6 (with optional DHCPv6 package)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1030">Os dois primeiros métodos são descritos abaixo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1030">The first two methods are described below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1031">O 3º método (DHCPv6) está descrito no pacote DHCP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1031">The 3rd method (DHCPv6) is described in the DHCP package.</span></span>

### <a name="stateless-address-autoconfiguration-using-router-solicitation"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1032">Configuração automática de endereço apátrida usando solicitação do router</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1032">Stateless Address Autoconfiguration Using Router Solicitation</span></span>      
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1033">Os dispositivos NetX Duo podem configurar automaticamente as suas interfaces quando ligados a uma rede IPv6 com um router que fornece informações prefixos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1033">NetX Duo devices can configure their interfaces automatically when connected to an IPv6 network with a router that supplies prefix information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1034">Os dispositivos que requerem configuração automática de endereços apátridas enviam mensagens de solicitação de router (RS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1034">Devices that require Stateless Address Autoconfiguration send out router solicitation (RS) messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1035">Os routers na rede respondem com mensagens de publicidade de router solicitadas (RA).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1035">Routers on the network respond with solicited router advertisement (RA) messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1036">As mensagens RA anunciam prefixos que identificam os endereços de rede associados a um link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1036">RA messages advertise prefixes that identify the network addresses associated with a link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1037">Os dispositivos geram então um identificador único para a rede a que o dispositivo está ligado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1037">Devices then generate a unique identifier for the network the device is attached to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1038">O endereço é formado combinando o prefixo e o seu identificador único.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1038">The address is formed by combining the prefix and its unique identifier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1039">Desta forma, ao receber as mensagens RA, os anfitriões geram o seu endereço IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1039">In this manner on receiving the RA messages, hosts generate their IP address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1040">Os routers também podem enviar mensagens DE RA não solicitadas periódicas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1040">Routers may also send periodic unsolicited RA messages.</span></span> 

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1041">*O NetX Duo permite uma aplicação para ativar ou desativar a configuração automática do endereço apátrida no tempo de execução. Para ativar esta funcionalidade, a biblioteca NetX Duo deve ser compilada com **NX_IPV6_STATELESS_AUTOCONFIG_CONTROL** definida. Uma vez ativada esta funcionalidade, as aplicações podem utilizar **nxd_ipv6_stateless_address_autoconfigure_enable** e **nxd_ipv6_stateless_address_autocofigure_disable** para ativar ou desativar o endereço apátrida IPv6 automaticamente configurar*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1041">*NetX Duo allows an application to enable or disable Stateless Address Autoconfiguration at run time. To enable this feature, NetX Duo library must be compiled with **NX_IPV6_STATELESS_AUTOCONFIG_CONTROL** defined. Once this feature is enabled, applications may use **nxd_ipv6_stateless_address_autoconfigure_enable** and **nxd_ipv6_stateless_address_autocofigure_disable** to enable or disable IPv6 stateless address autoconfiguration*.</span></span>

### <a name="manual-ipv6-address-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1042">Configuração manual do endereço IPv6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1042">Manual IPv6 Address Configuration</span></span>     
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1043">Se for necessário um endereço IPv6 específico, a aplicação poderá utilizar ***nxd_ipv6_address_set*** para configurar manualmente um endereço IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1043">If a specific IPv6 address is needed, the application may use ***nxd_ipv6_address_set*** to manually configure an IPv6 address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1044">Uma interface de rede pode ter vários endereços IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1044">A network interface may have multiple IPv6 addresses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1045">No entanto, tenha em mente que o número total de endereços IPv6 num sistema, obtido através da configuração automática do endereço apátrida, ou através da Configuração Manual, não pode exceder ***NX_MAX_IPV6_ADDRESSES***.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1045">However keep in mind that the total number of IPv6 addresses in a system, either obtained through Stateless Address Autoconfiguration, or through the Manual Configuration, cannot exceed ***NX_MAX_IPV6_ADDRESSES***.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1046">O exemplo a seguir ilustra como configurar manualmente um endereço global na interface primária (dispositivo 0) em ip_0:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1046">The following example illustrates how to manually configure a global address on the primary interface (device 0) in ip_0:</span></span>

```c
NXD_ADDRESS global_address;
global_address.nxd_ip_version = NX_IP_VERSION_V6;
global_address.nxd_ip_address.v6[0] = 0x20010000;
global_address.nxd_ip_address.v6[1] = 0x00000000;
global_address.nxd_ip_address.v6[2] = 0x00000000;
global_address.nxd_ip_address.v6[3] = 0x0000ABCD;
```

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1047">Em seguida, o anfitrião chama o seguinte serviço NetX Duo para atribuir este endereço como o seu endereço IP global:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1047">The host then calls the following NetX Duo service to assign this address as its global IP address:</span></span>

```c
status = nxd_ipv6_address_set(&ip_0, 0,  
                              &global_address, 64
                              NX_NULL);
```

### <a name="duplicate-address-detection-dad"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1048">Deteção de endereços duplicado (DAD)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1048">Duplicate Address Detection (DAD)</span></span>    
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1049">Depois de um sistema configurar o seu endereço IPv6, o endereço é marcado como *PROVISÓRIO*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1049">After a system configures its IPv6 address, the address is marked as *TENTATIVE*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1050">Se a Duplicado Deteção de Endereços (DAD), descrita no RFC 4862, estiver ativada, a NetX Duo envia automaticamente mensagens de solicitação de vizinhos (NS) com este endereço provisório como destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1050">If Duplicate Address Detection (DAD), described in RFC 4862, is enabled, NetX Duo automatically sends neighbor solicitation (NS) messages with this tentative address as the destination.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1051">Se nenhum anfitrião na rede responder a estas mensagens NS num determinado período de tempo, o endereço é assumido como único na ligação local, e o seu estado transita para o estado VÁLIDO.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1051">If no hosts on the network respond to these NS messages within a given period of time, the address is assumed to be unique on the local link, and its state transits to the VALID state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1052">Neste momento, a aplicação pode começar a utilizar este endereço IP para comunicação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1052">At this point the application may start using this IP address for communication.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1053">A funcionalidade DAD faz parte do módulo ICMPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1053">The DAD functionality is part of the ICMPv6 module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1054">Por isso, a aplicação deve permitir serviços ICMPv6 antes que um endereço recém-configurado possa passar pelo processo DAD.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1054">Therefore, the application must enable ICMPv6 services before a newly configured address can go through the DAD process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1055">Alternativamente, o processo DAD pode ser desligado definindo ***NX_DISABLE_IPV6_DAD** _ opção no ambiente de construção da biblioteca NetX Duo (definido como _*_nx_user.h)._\*_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1055">Alternatively, the DAD process may be turned off by defining ***NX_DISABLE_IPV6_DAD** _ option in the NetX Duo library build environment (defined as _*_nx_user.h_\*_).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1056">Durante o processo DAD, o parâmetro _*_NX_IPV6_DAD_TRANSMITS_*_ determina o número de mensagens NS enviadas pela NetX Duo sem receber uma resposta para determinar que o endereço é único.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1056">During the DAD process, the _*_NX_IPV6_DAD_TRANSMITS_*_ parameter determines the number of NS messages sent by NetX Duo without receiving a response to determine that the address is unique.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1057">Por predefinição e recomendado pelo RFC 4862, _ *_NX_IPV6_DAD_TRANSMITS_*\* é definido em 3.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1057">By default and recommended by RFC 4862, _ *_NX_IPV6_DAD_TRANSMITS_*\* is set at 3.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1058">Definir este símbolo a zero desativa eficazmente o PAI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1058">Setting this symbol to zero effectively disables DAD.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1059">Se o ICMPv6 ou o DAD não estiverem ativados no momento em que a aplicação atribuir um endereço IPv6, o DAD não é realizado e o NetX Duo define imediatamente o estado do endereço IPv6 para VALID.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1059">If ICMPv6 or DAD is not enabled at the time the application assigns an IPv6 address, DAD is not performed and NetX Duo sets the state of the IPv6 address to VALID immediately.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1060">A NetX Duo não pode comunicar na rede IPv6 até que o seu endereço local e/ou global seja válido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1060">NetX Duo cannot communicate on the IPv6 network until its link local and/or global address is valid.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1061">Após a obtenção de um endereço válido, o NetX Duo tenta combinar o endereço de destino de um pacote de entrada com um dos seus endereços IPv6 configurados ou um endereço multicast ativado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1061">After a valid address is obtained, NetX Duo attempts to match the destination address of an incoming packet against one of its configured IPv6 address or an enabled multicast address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1062">Se não forem encontrados fósforos, o pacote é retirado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1062">If no matches are found, the packet is dropped.</span></span> 

> [!WARNING]  
> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1063">\*Durante o processo DAD, o número de pacotes DAD NS a transmitir é definido por \***NX_IPV6_DAD_TRANSMITS,**_que não chega a 3, e por padrão há um atraso de um segundo entre cada mensagem DAD NS é enviado. Portanto, num sistema com o PAI ativado, depois de atribuído um endereço IPv6 (e assumindo que este não é um endereço duplicado), há aproximadamente 3 segundos de atraso antes do endereço IP estar em estado VÁLIDO e estar pronto para comunicação._</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1063">\*During the DAD process, the number of DAD NS packets to be transmitted is defined by \***NX_IPV6_DAD_TRANSMITS**_, which defaults to 3, and by default there is a one second delay between each DAD NS message is sent. Therefore, in a system with DAD enabled, after an IPv6 address is assigned (and assuming this is not a duplicated address), there is approximately 3 seconds delay before the IP address is in a VALID state and is ready for communication._</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1064">As aplicações podem querer receber notificações quando os endereços IPv6 no sistema forem alterados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1064">Applications may want to receive notifications when IPv6 addresses in the system are changed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1065">Para ativar a funcionalidade de notificação de alteração de endereço IPv6, a biblioteca NetX Duo deve ser construída com o símbolo **NX_ENABLE_IPV6_ADDRESS_CHANGE_NOTIFY** definido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1065">To enable the IPv6 address change notification feature, the NetX Duo library must be built with the symbol **NX_ENABLE_IPV6_ADDRESS_CHANGE_NOTIFY** defined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1066">Uma vez ativada a função, as aplicações podem instalar a função de retorno utilizando o serviço **_nxd_ipv6_address_change_notify._**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1066">Once the feature is enabled, applications may install the callback function by using the **_nxd_ipv6_address_change_notify_** service.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1067">Uma vez que um endereço IPv6 é alterado ou se torna inválido, a função de retorno fornecida pelo utilizador é invocada com as seguintes informações:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1067">Once an IPv6 address is changed, or becomes invalid, the user-supplied callback function is invoked with the following information:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1068">Função</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1068">Function</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1069">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1069">Description</span></span>  |
|---|---|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1070">ip_ptr</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1070">ip_ptr</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1071">Ponteiro para a instância IP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1071">Pointer to the IP instance</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1072">interface_index</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1072">interface_index</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1073">Índice para a interface de rede que este endereço IPv6 está associado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1073">Index to the network interface that this IPv6 address is associated with</span></span>
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1074">ipv6_addr_index</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1074">ipv6_addr_index</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1075">Índice para a tabela de endereços IPv6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1075">Index to the IPv6 address table</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1076">ipv6_address</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1076">ipv6_address</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1077">Ponteiro para o endereço IPv6, na forma de uma matriz de quatro inteiros ULONG.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1077">Pointer to the IPv6 address, in the form of an array of four ULONG integers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1078">Os endereços Pv6 são apresentados em ordem byte de anfitrião.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1078">Pv6 addresses are presented in host byte order.</span></span>|

### <a name="ipv6-multicast-support-in-netx-duo"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1079">Suporte multicast IPv6 na NetX Duo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1079">IPv6 Multicast Support In NetX Duo</span></span>      
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1080">Os endereços multicast especificam um grupo dinâmico de anfitriões na Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1080">Multicast addresses specify a dynamic group of hosts on the Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1081">Os membros do grupo multicast podem juntar-se e sair quando quiserem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1081">Members of the multicast group may join and leave whenever they wish.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1082">A NetX Duo implementa vários protocolos ICMPv6, incluindo duplicado deteção de endereços, descoberta de vizinhos e discovery router, que requerem capacidade multicast IP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1082">NetX Duo implements several ICMPv6 protocols, including Duplicate Address Detection, Neighbor Discovery, and Router Discovery, which require IP multicast capability.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1083">Por isso, a NetX Duo espera que o controlador do dispositivo subjacente suporte operações multicast.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1083">Therefore, NetX Duo expects the underlying device driver to support multicast operations.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1084">Quando o NetX Duo precisa de se juntar ou sair de um grupo multicast (como o endereço multicast all-node e o endereço multicast *de nó solicitado),* emite um comando do controlador ao controlador do dispositivo para se juntar ou deixar um endereço MAC multicast.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1084">When NetX Duo needs to join or leave a multicast group (such as the all-node multicast address, and the *solicited-node* multicast address), it issues a driver command to the device driver to join or leave a multicast MAC address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1085">O comando do controlador para se juntar ao endereço multicast é \***NX_LINK_MULTICAST_JOIN** _.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1085">The driver command for joining the multicast address is \***NX_LINK_MULTICAST_JOIN** _.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1086">Para deixar um endereço multicast, a NetX Duo emite o comando do controlador _\*_NX_LINK_MULTICAST_LEAVE_\*\*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1086">To leave a multicast address, NetX Duo issues the driver command _\*_NX_LINK_MULTICAST_LEAVE_\*\*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1087">O controlador do dispositivo deve implementar estes dois comandos para que os protocolos ICMPv6 funcionem corretamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1087">The device driver must implement these two commands for ICMPv6 protocols to work properly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1088">As aplicações podem aderir a um grupo multicast IPv6 utilizando o serviço \***nxd_ipv6_multicast_interface_join\*.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1088">Applications may join an IPv6 multicast group by using the service \***nxd_ipv6_multicast_interface_join\*.**</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1089">Este serviço regista o endereço multicast com a pilha IP e, em seguida, notifica o controlador de dispositivo especificado do endereço multicast IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1089">This service registers the multicast address with the IP stack, and then notifies the specified device driver of the IPv6 multicast address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1090">Para deixar um grupo multicast, as aplicações utilizam o ***serviço nxd_ipv6_multicast_interface_leave.***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1090">To leave a multicast group, applications use the service ***nxd_ipv6_multicast_interface_leave.***</span></span>

### <a name="neighbor-discovery-nd"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1091">Neighbor Discovery (ND)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1091">Neighbor Discovery (ND)</span></span>    
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1092">Neighbor Discovery é um protocolo em redes IPv6 para mapear endereços físicos para os endereços IPv6 (endereço global ou endereço link-local).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1092">Neighbor Discovery is a protocol in IPv6 networks for mapping physical addresses to the IPv6 addresses (global address or link-local address).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1093">Este mapeamento é mantido na Cache de Descoberta do Vizinho (Cache ND).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1093">This mapping is maintained in the Neighbor Discovery Cache (ND Cache).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1094">O processo ND é o equivalente ao processo ARP no IPv4, e a Cache ND é semelhante à tabela ARP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1094">The ND process is the equivalent of the ARP process in IPv4, and the ND Cache is similar to the ARP table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1095">Um nó IPv6 pode obter o endereço MAC do seu vizinho usando o protocolo Neighbor Discovery (ND).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1095">An IPv6 node can obtain its neighbor's MAC address using the Neighbor Discovery (ND) protocol.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1096">Envia uma mensagem de solicitação de vizinho (NS) para o endereço multicast de nó solicitado e aguarda uma mensagem de anúncio de vizinho correspondente (NA).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1096">It sends out a neighbor solicitation (NS) message to the all-node solicited node multicast address, and waits for a corresponding neighbor advertisement (NA) message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1097">O endereço MAC obtido através deste processo é armazenado na Cache ND.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1097">The MAC address obtained through this process is stored in the ND Cache.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1098">Cada instância IP tem uma cache ND.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1098">Each IP instance has one ND cache.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1099">A Cache ND é mantida como um conjunto de entradas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1099">The ND Cache is maintained as an array of entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1100">O tamanho da matriz é definido no tempo de compilação, definindo a opção ***NX_IPV6_NEIGHBOR_CACHE_SIZE** _ que em _*_nx_user.h\*\*._</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1100">The size of the array is defined at compilation time by setting the option ***NX_IPV6_NEIGHBOR_CACHE_SIZE** _ which in _*_nx_user.h_\*\*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1101">Note que todas as interfaces anexas a uma instância IP partilham a mesma cache ND.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1101">Note that all interfaces attached to an IP instance share the same ND cache.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1102">Toda a Cache ND está vazia quando o NetX Duo começar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1102">The entire ND Cache is empty when NetX Duo starts up.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1103">À medida que o sistema funciona, o NetX Duo atualiza automaticamente a Cache ND, adicionando e eliminando as entradas de acordo com o protocolo ND.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1103">As the system runs, NetX Duo automatically updates the ND Cache, adding and deleting entries as per ND protocol.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1104">No entanto, uma aplicação também pode atualizar o Cache ND adicionando e eliminando manualmente as entradas de cache utilizando os seguintes serviços NetX Duo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1104">However, an application may also update the ND Cache by manually adding and deleting cache entries using the following NetX Duo services:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1105">***nxd_nd_cache_entry_delete***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1105">***nxd_nd_cache_entry_delete***</span></span>  
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1106">***nxd_nd_cache_entry_set***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1106">***nxd_nd_cache_entry_set***</span></span>   
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1107">***nxd_nd_cache_invalidate***</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1107">***nxd_nd_cache_invalidate***</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1108">Ao enviar e receber pacotes IPv6, o NetX Duo atualiza automaticamente a tabela ND Cache.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1108">When sending and receiving IPv6 packets, NetX Duo automatically updates the ND Cache table.</span></span>

## <a name="internet-control-message-protocol-in-ipv6-icmpv6"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1109">Protocolo de mensagem de controlo da Internet em IPv6 (ICMPv6)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1109">Internet Control Message Protocol in IPv6 (ICMPv6)</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1110">O papel do ICMPv6 no IPv6 foi amplamente expandido para apoiar o mapeamento de endereços IPv6 e a descoberta do router.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1110">The role of ICMPv6 in IPv6 has been greatly expanded to support IPv6 address mapping and router discovery.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1111">Além disso, o NetX Duo ICMPv6 suporta pedido e resposta de eco, relatórios de erro ICMPv6 e mensagens de redirecionamento ICMPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1111">In addition, NetX Duo ICMPv6 supports echo request and response, ICMPv6 error reports, and ICMPv6 redirect messages.</span></span>

### <a name="icmpv6-enable"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1112">ICMPv6 Ativar</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1112">ICMPv6 Enable</span></span>    
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1113">Antes de as mensagens ICMPv6 poderem ser processadas pela NetX Duo, a aplicação deve ligar para o serviço ***nxd_icmp_enable*** para permitir o processamento do ICMPv6, conforme explicado anteriormente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1113">Before ICMPv6 messages can be processed by NetX Duo, the application must call the ***nxd_icmp_enable*** service to enable ICMPv6 processing as explained previously.</span></span> 

### <a name="icmpv6-messages"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1114">Mensagens ICMPv6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1114">ICMPv6 Messages</span></span>     
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1115">A estrutura do cabeçalho ICMPv6 é semelhante à estrutura do cabeçalho ICMPv4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1115">The ICMPv6 header structure is similar to the ICMPv4 header structure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1116">Como mostrado abaixo, o cabeçalho básico ICMPv6 contém os três campos, tipo, código e checkum, além do comprimento variável dos dados de opção ICMPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1116">As shown below, the basic ICMPv6 header contains the three fields, type, code, and checksum, plus variable length of ICMPv6 option data.</span></span> 

![Diagrama de um cabeçalho básico do ICMPv6.](./media/user-guide/image19.png)

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1118">**FIGURA 10. Cabeçalho Básico ICMPv6**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1118">**FIGURE 10. Basic ICMPv6 Header**</span></span>

|-----|-----|-----|
|     | <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1122">1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1122">1</span></span>   |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1123">Identifica o tipo de mensagem ICMPv6;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1123">Identifies the ICMPv6 message type;</span></span> |
|     |     |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1124">1 Destino Inacessível</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1124">1 Destination Unreachable</span></span> |
|     |     |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1125">2 Pacote Muito Grande</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1125">2 Packet Too Big</span></span> |
|     |     |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1126">3 Tempo Excedido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1126">3 Time Exceeded</span></span> |
|     |     |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1127">4 Problema de parâmetros</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1127">4 Parameter Problem</span></span> |
|     |     |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1128">128 Pedido de Eco</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1128">128 Echo Request</span></span> |
|     |     |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1129">129 Resposta de Eco</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1129">129 Echo Reply</span></span> |
|     |     |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1130">133 Solicitação do Router</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1130">133 Router Solicitation</span></span> |
|     |     |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1131">134 Anúncio de Router</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1131">134 Router Advertisement</span></span> |
|     |     |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1132">135 Solicitação de Vizinhos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1132">135 Neighbor Solicitation</span></span> |
|     |     |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1133">136 Anúncio do Vizinho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1133">136 Neighbor Advertisement</span></span> |
|     |     |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1134">137 Mensagem de Redirecionamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1134">137 Redirect Message</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1135">Código</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1135">Code</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1136">1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1136">1</span></span>   |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1137">Qualifica ainda o tipo de mensagem ICMPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1137">Further qualifies the ICMPv6 message type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1138">Geralmente usado com mensagens de erro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1138">Generally used with error messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1139">Se não for utilizado, está definido para zero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1139">If not used, it is set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1140">O pedido de eco/resposta e as mensagens NS não a utilizam.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1140">Echo request/reply and NS messages do not use it.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1141">Soma de verificação</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1141">Checksum</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1142">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1142">2</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1143">Campo de verificação de 16 bits para o cabeçalho ICMP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1143">16-bit checksum field for the ICMP Header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1144">Este é um complemento de 16 bits de toda a mensagem ICMPv6, incluindo o cabeçalho ICMPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1144">This is a 16-bit complement of the entire ICMPv6 message, including the ICMPv6 header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1145">Também inclui um pseudo-cabeçalho do endereço de origem IPv6, endereço de destino e comprimento de carga útil do pacote.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1145">It also includes a pseudo-header of the IPv6 source address, destination address, and packet payload length.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1146">Um exemplo do cabeçalho de solicitação do vizinho é mostrado abaixo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1146">An example Neighbor Solicitation header is shown below.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1152">Tipo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1152">Type</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1153">1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1153">1</span></span>   |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1154">Identifica o tipo de mensagem ICMPv6 para mensagens de solicitação de vizinhos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1154">Identifies the ICMPv6 message type for neighbor solicitation messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1155">O valor é 135.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1155">Value is 135.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1156">Código</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1156">Code</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1157">1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1157">1</span></span>   |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1158">Não usado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1158">Not used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1159">Pronto para 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1159">Set to 0.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1160">Soma de verificação</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1160">Checksum</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1161">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1161">2</span></span>  |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1162">Campo de verificação de 16 bits para o cabeçalho ICMPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1162">16-bit checksum field for the ICMPv6 header.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1163">Reservado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1163">Reserved</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1164">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1164">4</span></span>  |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1165">4 bytes reservados definidos para 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1165">4 reserved bytes set to 0.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1166">Endereço-alvo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1166">Target Address</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1167">16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1167">16</span></span>  |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1168">Endereço IPv6 do alvo da solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1168">IPv6 address of target of the solicitation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1169">Para a resolução de endereços IPv6, este é o endereço IP unicast real do dispositivo cujo endereço de camada de ligação precisa de ser resolvido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1169">For IPv6 address resolution, this is the actual unicast IP address of the device whose link layer address needs to be resolved.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1170">Opções</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1170">Options</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1171">Variável</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1171">Variable</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1172">Informação opcional especificada pelo Protocolo de Descoberta do Vizinho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1172">Optional information specified by the Neighbor Discovery Protocol.</span></span> |

### <a name="icmpv6-ping-request"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1173">Pedido de ping ICMPv6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1173">ICMPv6 Ping Request</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1174">Nas aplicações NetX Duo utilizam ***nxd_icmp_ping*** para emitir pedidos de ping IPv6 ou IPv4, com base no endereço IP de destino especificado nos parâmetros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1174">In NetX Duo applications use ***nxd_icmp_ping*** to issue either IPv6 or IPv4 ping requests, based on the destination IP address specified in the parameters.</span></span>  

### <a name="icmpv6-ping-response"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1175">Resposta ao ping ICMPv6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1175">ICMPv6 Ping Response</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1176">Uma resposta de ping ICMPv6 é outro tipo de mensagem ICMPv6 que é gerada internamente pela componente ICMPv6 em resposta a um pedido externo de ping ICMPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1176">An ICMPv6 ping response is another type of ICMPv6 message that is generated internally by the ICMPv6 component in response to an external ICMPv6 ping request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1177">Além do reconhecimento, a resposta ao ping ICMPv6 contém também uma cópia dos dados do utilizador fornecidos no pedido de ping do ICMPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1177">In additional to acknowledgement, the ICMPv6 ping response also contains a copy of the user data supplied in the ICMPv6 ping request.</span></span>  

### <a name="thread-suspension"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1178">Suspensão do fio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1178">Thread Suspension</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1179">Os fios de aplicação podem ser suspensos enquanto tentam pingar outro membro da rede.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1179">Application threads can suspend while attempting to ping another network member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1180">Após a resposta ao ping ser recebida, a mensagem de resposta do ping é dada ao primeiro fio suspenso e esse fio é retomado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1180">After a ping response is received, the ping response message is given to the first thread suspended and that thread is resumed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1181">Como todos os serviços da NetX Duo, suspender um pedido de ping tem um tempo limite opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1181">Like all NetX Duo services, suspending on a ping request has an optional timeout.</span></span>  

### <a name="other-icmpv6-messages"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1182">Outras mensagens ICMPv6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1182">Other ICMPv6 Messages</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1183">São necessárias mensagens ICMPv6 para as seguintes funcionalidades:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1183">ICMPv6 messages are required for the following features:</span></span>  

- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1184">Descoberta do Vizinho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1184">Neighbor Discovery</span></span>  
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1185">Autoconfiguação de endereço apátrida</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1185">Stateless Address Autoconfiguration</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1186">Descoberta do Router</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1186">Router Discovery</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1187">Deteção de Inacessibilidade do Vizinho</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1187">Neighbor Unreachability Detection</span></span>  

### <a name="neighbor-unreachability-router-and-prefix-discovery"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1188">Inalabilidade do vizinho, router e prefix discovery</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1188">Neighbor Unreachability, Router and Prefix Discovery</span></span>    
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1189">Neighbor Unreachability Detection, Router Discovery e Prefix Discovery são baseados no protocolo Neighbor Discovery e são descritos abaixo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1189">Neighbor Unreachability Detection, Router Discovery, and Prefix Discovery are based on the Neighbor Discovery protocol and are described below.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1190">***Deteção de Inacessibilidade do Vizinho:*** Um dispositivo IPv6 procura a cache da Neighbor Discovery (ND) para o endereço da camada de ligação de destino quando deseja enviar um pacote.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1190">***Neighbor Unreachability Detection:*** An IPv6 device searches its Neighbor Discovery (ND) Cache for the destination link layer address when it wishes to send a packet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1191">O destino imediato, por vezes referido como o "próximo salto", pode ser o destino real no mesmo link ou pode ser um router se o destino estiver fora de ligação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1191">The immediate destination, sometimes referred to as the 'next hop,' may be the actual destination on the same link or it may be a router if the destination is off link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1192">Uma entrada de cache ND contém o estado na capacidade de alcance de um vizinho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1192">An ND cache entry contains the status on a neighbor's reachability.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1193">Um estado de alcance indica que o vizinho é considerado acessível.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1193">A REACHABLE status indicates the neighbor is considered reachable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1194">Um vizinho está contactável se recebeu recentemente a confirmação de que os pacotes enviados para o vizinho foram recebidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1194">A neighbor is reachable if it has recently received confirmation that packets sent to the neighbor have been received.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1195">A confirmação no NetX Duo assume a forma de receber uma mensagem NA do vizinho em resposta a uma mensagem NS enviada pelo dispositivo NetX Duo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1195">Confirmation in NetX Duo take the form of receiving an NA message from the neighbor in response to an NS message sent by the NetX Duo device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1196">A NetX Duo também alterará o estado do estado do vizinho para REACHABLE se a aplicação ligar para o serviço NetX Duo ***nxd_nd_cache_entry_set*** para introduzir manualmente um registo de cache.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1196">NetX Duo will also change the state of the neighbor status to REACHABLE if the application calls the NetX Duo service ***nxd_nd_cache_entry_set*** to manually enter a cache record.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1197">***Descoberta do Router:*** Um dispositivo IPv6 utiliza um router para encaminhar todos os pacotes destinados a destinos fora de ligação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1197">***Router Discovery:*** An IPv6 device uses a router to forward all packets intended for off link destinations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1198">Pode também utilizar informações enviadas pelo router, como mensagens de publicidade de router (RA), para configurar os seus endereços IPv6 globais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1198">It may also use information sent by the router, such as router advertisement (RA) messages, to configure its global IPv6 addresses.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1199">Um dispositivo na rede pode iniciar o processo de Discovery router enviando uma mensagem de solicitação de router (RS) para o endereço multicast de todos os routers (FF01::2).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1199">A device on the network may initiate the Router Discovery process by sending a router solicitation (RS) message to the all-router multicast address (FF01::2).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1200">Ou pode esperar no endereço multicast de todos os nós (FF::1) para um RA periódico dos routers.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1200">Or it can wait on the all-node multicast address (FF::1) for a periodic RA from the routers.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1201">Uma mensagem RA contém as informações de prefixo para configurar um endereço IPv6 para essa rede.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1201">An RA message contains the prefix information for configuring an IPv6 address for that network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1202">No NetX Duo, a solicitação do router está por defeito ativada e pode ser desativada definindo a opção de configuração ***NX_DISABLE_ICMPV6_ROUTER_SOLICITATION** _ em _*_nx_user.h_\*\*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1202">In NetX Duo, router solicitation is by default enabled and can be disabled by setting the configuration option ***NX_DISABLE_ICMPV6_ROUTER_SOLICITATION** _ in _*_nx_user.h_\*\*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1203">Consulte as opções de configuração no capítulo "Instalação e Utilização da NetX Duo" para obter mais detalhes sobre a definição dos parâmetros de solicitação do router.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1203">See Configuration Options in the "Installation and Use of NetX Duo" chapter for more details on setting Router Solicitation parameters.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1204">***Prefix Discovery***: Um dispositivo IPv6 utiliza a descoberta do prefixo para saber quais os anfitriões-alvo que estão acessíveis diretamente sem passar por um router.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1204">***Prefix Discovery***: An IPv6 device uses prefix discovery to learn which target hosts are accessible directly without going through a router.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1205">Estas informações são disponibilizadas ao dispositivo IPv6 a partir de mensagens RA do router.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1205">This information is made available to the IPv6 device from RA messages from the router.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1206">O dispositivo IPv6 armazena a informação do prefixo numa tabela de prefixos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1206">The IPv6 device stores the prefix information in a prefix table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1207">A descoberta do prefixo corresponde a um prefixo do prefixo do dispositivo IPv6 com um endereço alvo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1207">Prefix discovery is matching a prefix from the IPv6 device prefix table to a target address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1208">Um prefixo corresponde a um endereço-alvo se todos os bits do prefixo corresponderem às partes mais significativas do endereço alvo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1208">A prefix matches a target address if all the bits in the prefix match the most significant bits of the target address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1209">Se mais de um prefixo cobrir um endereço, o prefixo mais longo é selecionado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1209">If more than one prefix covers an address, the longest prefix is selected.</span></span>

### <a name="icmpv6-error-messages"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1210">Mensagens de erro ICMPv6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1210">ICMPv6 Error Messages</span></span>    
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1211">As seguintes mensagens de erro ICMPv6 são suportadas no NetX Duo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1211">The following ICMPv6 error messages are supported in NetX Duo:</span></span>  

- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1212">Destino Inacessível</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1212">Destination Unreachable</span></span>  
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1213">Pacote muito grande</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1213">Packet Too Big</span></span>  
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1214">Exceder o tempo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1214">Time Exceed</span></span>  
- <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1215">Problema de parâmetros</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1215">Parameter Problem</span></span>  

## <a name="user-datagram-protocol-udp"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1216">Protocolo de Datagrama do Utilizador (UDP)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1216">User Datagram Protocol (UDP)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1217">O Protocolo de Datagrama do Utilizador (UDP) fornece a forma mais simples de transferência de dados entre membros da rede (RFC 768).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1217">The User Datagram Protocol (UDP) provides the simplest form of data transfer between network members (RFC 768).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1218">Os pacotes de dados da UDP são enviados de um membro da rede para outro da melhor forma de esforço; ou seja, não existe um mecanismo incorporado para reconhecimento pelo destinatário do pacote.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1218">UDP data packets are sent from one network member to another in a best effort fashion; i.e., there is no built-in mechanism for acknowledgement by the packet recipient.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1219">Além disso, o envio de um pacote UDP não requer qualquer ligação a ser estabelecida antecipadamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1219">In addition, sending a UDP packet does not require any connection to be established in advance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1220">Por causa disso, a transmissão de pacotes da UDP é muito eficiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1220">Because of this, UDP packet transmission is very efficient.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1221">Para os desenvolvedores que migram as suas aplicações NetX para o NetX Duo existem apenas algumas alterações básicas na funcionalidade UDP entre NetX e NetX Duo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1221">For developers migrating their NetX applications to NetX Duo there are only a few basic changes in UDP functionality between NetX and NetX Duo.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1222">Isto porque o IPv6 se preocupa principalmente com a camada ip subjacente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1222">This is because IPv6 is primarily concerned with the underlying IP layer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1223">Todos os serviços netx Duo UDP podem ser usados para conectividade IPv4 ou IPv6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1223">All NetX Duo UDP services can be used for either IPv4 or IPv6 connectivity.</span></span>

### <a name="udp-header"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1224">Cabeçalho UDP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1224">UDP Header</span></span>       
<span data-ttu-id="15c79-1225">A UDP coloca um simples cabeçalho de pacote na frente dos dados da aplicação sobre a transmissão, e remove um cabeçalho UDP semelhante do pacote na receção antes de entregar um pacote UDP recebido à aplicação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1225">UDP places a simple packet header in front of the application's data on transmission, and removes a similar UDP header from the packet on reception before delivering a received UDP packet to the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1226">O UDP utiliza o protocolo IP para o envio e receção de pacotes, o que significa que há um cabeçalho IP em frente ao cabeçalho da UDP quando o pacote está na rede.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1226">UDP utilizes the IP protocol for sending and receiving packets, which means there is an IP header in front of the UDP header when the packet is on the network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1227">A figura 12 mostra o formato do cabeçalho UDP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1227">Figure 12 shows the format of the UDP header.</span></span>

![Diagrama do formato do cabeçalho da UDP.](./media/user-guide/image21.png)

### <a name="figure-12-udp-header"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c79-1229">FIGURA 12.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1229">FIGURE 12.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c79-1230">Cabeçalho UDP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c79-1230">UDP Header</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
